```
Downtime Projects
```

Research Projects

Heroes can undertake many different types of research downtime
projects, which can involve procurar out new lore, improving existing
Conhecimento with study, uncovering Boatos or secrets, and more.

Unless a project has a event table of its own or a Especial event entry,
the Diretor uses the Crafting and Research Events table for research
project events.

**Discover Lore**

**Item Pré-requisito:** Nenhuma
**Origem do Projeto:** Texts or Conhecimento related to the subject you
wish to research
**Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic:** Razão
**Objetivo de Projeto:** Varies (see the table)

If you want to Rastrear the location of a lost Tesouro, decipher a ritual, or
trace the lineage of a royal family to find the next heir to the throne,
you can start a Projeto de Tempo Livre to delve into whatever mysteries you
seek to unravel. You Músculo start a project to discover lore because the
information can’t be discovered through a single Teste, or you could do so
because you failed a Teste to Recolher information and now want to learn it
through research.

When you start a Projeto de Tempo Livre to discover lore, you choose the
lore you want investigated and the questions you want answered. The
Diretor tells you if the lore you seek amounts to common, obscure,
lost, or forbidden Conhecimento. The more esoteric the Conhecimento, the
more project points are required to find the answers you seek.

```
Discover Lore Project Goals
Objetivo de Projeto
Common Conhecimento 15
Obscure Conhecimento 45
Lost Conhecimento 120
Forbidden Conhecimento 240
```

Common Conhecimento
Common Conhecimento is generally easy to discover with a day or so of
research. It’s not known by every passerby and takes time to uncover,
but with plentiful local sources for the information, you don’t need
to Gastar a lot of time searching. It could be that you need to question
several members of a rumor mill to figure out who a Nobre is not-so-se-
cretly courting, or you Músculo need to Gastar a few hours in a temple to
find the particular religious text that carries a seldom-used alternative
name for a deity.

```
Obscure Conhecimento
Obscure Conhecimento is known only to specialized sages and is typically
of Interesse only to those scholars. As such, precious few tomes are
written on obscure subjects. Finding the right expert to interview
or the best book to read typically requires several days of research.
Uncovering the details of a ritual used to Receptivo and close a portal to the
Sea of Stars isn’t easy information to come by, but there are people out
there who know how to do it—and who wrote the instructions down.
```

```
Lost Conhecimento
Lost Conhecimento is so esoteric that even among a field’s most dedicated
scholars, there Músculo be only um or dois individuals who have dug
deep enough to know that lore. Lost Conhecimento could come from a
time so long ago that only a single text in a dead idioma now holds
the lore you seek. Such lore often takes more than a week to hunt
down. The location of a legendary steel Anão ’s workshop is most likely
lore that is lost—except for um map Escondida in a private collection.
```

```
Forbidden Conhecimento
Forbidden Conhecimento is lore that a powerful individual or Organização
is attempting to keep secret. Those who know the secrets speak of
them in whispered codes after passwords are exchanged, and write
texts using ciphers. Hunting down leads and making sense of them
typically takes weeks. The location of the dagger that slit the throat of
the god of Morte is Escondida behind layers of encoded text and written in
a dead idioma known only to that god’s most devout followers.
```

```
d100 Event
```

```
01–02
```

```
After the roll, a thief who wants the Origem do Projeto or an item needed for the
project approaches the Herói and pretends to be someone who wants to help.
The thief Músculo want to sell the Origem do Projeto or item, or use it to undertake
the same project as the Herói.
```

```
03–04
```

```
Before the roll, a traveler in need of food, shelter, or some other necessity
happens upon the heroes and asks for their help. If the heroes show kindness,
the traveler reveals themself to be an Artesão or Sábio who can help with the
project. The traveler can contribute um Lançamento de Projeto to the project with a +3
Modificador.
```

```
05–06
```

```
Before the roll, an NPC who is already Amigável with the characters and has
helped them before asks the Herói to let them join the project. The NPC
explains that they need the Origem do Projeto or the objeto being crafted for a
personal matter of great importance (saving someone’s Vida, righting a great
wrong, and so forth). The NPC can contribute um Lançamento de Projeto to the project
with a +3 Modificador, but the characters must commit to letting the NPC use the
finished project before they can do so.
```

```
07–08
```

```
After the roll, the Herói receives a mysterious note from a person who wants to
Mercado a Tesouro or other Recompensa for the Origem do Projeto when the project
is complete. The buyer could be someone with their own Interesse in a similar
project, an inimigo eager to exploit what the Herói is working on, or a superfan
who wants to emulate the Herói.
```

```
09–10
```

```
Before the roll, a pest starts devouring important components of the project.
This could be rats gnawing at alchemical components, moths eating rare silks,
mites devouring a printed Origem do Projeto, and so forth. If the pests aren’t dealt
with quickly, some of the components will need to be replaced.
```

```
11–12
```

```
Before the roll, a powerful Sobrenatural entity sends an Agente or premonition
to the Herói, offering them Conhecimento that will let them complete the project
immediately. In Mercado, the Herói must agree to do a favor for the entity,
which Músculo not be specified at the time of the bargain.
```

```
13–14
```

```
Before the roll, a rumor arises that the project is being worked on in service to
an evil entity. People start showing up to the Herói’s place of Descanso, demanding
that they repent their wicked ways. If the Boatos aren’t disproved, locals form
a Gangue to stop the project.
```

```
15–16
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói’s Rival comes to visit and shows off a Guia for the
project. The Rival is willing to hand the Guia over ... provided the Herói publicly
humiliates themself by proclaiming that the Rival is their better.
```

```
17–18
```

```
The Origem do Projeto is Amaldiçoado. Before the roll, the Herói must succeed on a
hard Intuição Teste or become obsessed with the project. Until the project is
complete, the Herói can’t use Victories to increase their Recurso Heróico. The
curse can be broken by slaying the criatura who bestowed it, or by finding a
priest to perform a Sagrado ritual over the Origem do Projeto.
```

```
19–20
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói finds that a significant amount of the project has been
completed by a group of fairies. The fairies Músculo have completed the job out of
boredom, or they Músculo want something from the Herói in return.
```

```
21–22
```

```
After the roll, the Herói realizes that the Origem do Projeto contains only half the
information they need, and they must find the rest of the information to
complete the project.
```

```
23–24
```

```
After the roll, the Herói discovers a new bit of Conhecimento or a technique that
allows them to immediately start and finish a second project with a project
goal of 50 or lower.
```

```
25–26
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói finds that someone has attempted to Sabotar
their project, resulting in dano to notes, the Origem do Projeto, or crafting
components. The dano is negligible, but the criatura responsible will Golpe
De Novo to worse Efeito if not discovered.
```

```
27–28
```

```
Before the roll, the Origem do Projeto is found to hold additional information,
letting the Herói treat the Lançamento de Projeto as an automatic Avanço. The note
could have been left by a helpful visitor, or by someone who wants the Herói’s
work to be finished for their own gain.
```

```
29–30
```

```
After the roll, the project draws the attention of a Diabo, who tries to subtly
change the Origem do Projeto from As Sete Cidades do Inferno. If the Herói doesn’t
notice, the Diabo is summoned the next time the Herói makes a Lançamento de Projeto, with
goals of the Diretor’s Determinação.
```

```
31–32
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói stumbles upon a tool, expert, or book that helps
them with the project, letting them treat the Lançamento de Projeto as an automatic
Avanço.
```

```
33–34
```

```
After the roll, the Origem do Projeto suddenly becomes impossible to understand.
A Psiônica NPC has used a mighty Poder to obscure or corrupt the project
source to prevent a potential catastrophe they foresaw. If the heroes can help
prevent the catastrophe in another way, the NPC will end the Efeito.
35–36 After the roll, the Herói discovers that the Origem do Projeto contains a piece of helpful Conhecimento unrelated to the current project.
```

d100 Event
```

```
37–38
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói learns that several sages working on similar projects
have all mysteriously disappeared. Someone or something is abducting these
experts for some nefarious purpose ... and the Herói could be next!
```

```
39–40
```

```
After the roll, a group of scholars approach the Herói and ask if they can review
the Origem do Projeto, promising to help the Herói complete the project in return. If
the Herói accepts, the scholars take the Origem do Projeto until the end of the Herói’s
next Descanso. três of the scholars then contribute project rolls during the
following Descanso, each with a +3 Modificador.
```

```
41–42
```

```
After the roll, a physical Origem do Projeto or crafting components come to Vida and
attack the Herói. Magia within these items has become corrupted! If the Herói
can fix the Corrupção without destroying the items, the project is saved, but
doing so requires a Especial ritual.
```

```
43–44
```

```
After the roll, an otherworldly Espectro appears and warns the Herói not to
complete the project, explaining that they died attempting the same project
and are now attached to the Origem do Projeto. If the Herói can convince the
spirit that they will not die similarly, the criatura shares their Conhecimento,
contributing um Lançamento de Projeto to the project with a +3 Modificador.
```

```
45–46
```

```
Before the roll, the servants of a Dragão appear and demand that the Herói hand
over the Origem do Projeto. If the Herói refuses, the servants warn that the Dragão
will come to claim the Origem do Projeto for themself.
```

```
47–48
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói notices a contract written on a physical Origem do Projeto
or other accompanying materials that appears only under certain conditions
(in the Presença of Magia, in the Luz of a full moon, and so forth). The contract
promises that anyone who signs it in blood will receive the true and full
answer to três questions, in Mercado for a week of service to the Bruxa Corrine
Withersnipe. The Bruxa appears instantly if the contract is signed.
```

```
49–50
```

```
After the roll, an unexpected total Eclipse of the Sol occurs, lasting 1 hour.
Once per Descanso when qualquer criatura makes another Lançamento de Projeto for the project,
another Eclipse occurs and lasts twice as long as the previous. Some take this
phenomenon as a sign of impending Ruína that will descend when the project
is completed. Others believe that a powerful inimigo is trying to scare the
heroes into not finishing the project.
```

```
51–52
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói gets a visit from an NPC who they helped in the past.
The NPC has found a Guia that relates to the project and gives it to the Herói as
a gift of thanks.
```

```
53–54
```

```
After the roll, a local officer of the law appears and tells the Herói to stop
working on their project. The Natureza of the Herói’s project has just become
outlawed in the region, and the constable insists on locking up the project
source and arresting anyone who gets in the way.
```

```
55–56
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói determines that the research or crafting they are
planning requires only part of their attention. They can either make dois
project rolls for their current project, or can make um for that project and um
for another project.
```

```
57–58
```

```
After the roll, a component or tool the Herói is using for the project suddenly
reveals itself to be Magia or Psiônica as it starts to hum with energy and glow
red hot. If the item isn’t quickly cooled, it explodes, and work on the project
can’t continue until a replacement is found.
```

```
59–60
```

```
Before the roll, the Herói realizes they’re at a critical point in the project, and can
achieve more if they just shave off a few hours of rest. By choosing to lose some
sleep, the personagem can make dois project rolls for the project, but when they
end the current Descanso, they do so with 1 fewer Recoveries than usual.
```

```
61–62
```

```
Before the roll, a Sábio approaches the Herói and offers to help with the project.
This NPC isn’t really a Sábio, however—they’re an Assassino hoping to catch the
Herói off Guarda.
```

```
63–64
```

```
Before the roll, a Sábio approaches the Herói and offers to help with the project.
This NPC isn’t really a Sábio, however—they’re a bard who wishes to compose
a song about the Herói’s deeds. The Is to ingratiate themself to the Herói while
contributing nothing to the actual project.
```

```
65–66
```

```
After the roll, a physical Origem do Projeto or a component of the project creates
an unstable portal to another world related to the Natureza of the project. Tiny
devils, elementals, or other criaturas start clawing their way out of the item
and causing mischief.
```

```
67–68
```

```
After the roll, the Herói realizes that the Origem do Projeto also holds information
regarding the location of another Origem do Projeto or certain items, which are
needed for another project the Herói or um of their aliados wants to pursue.
```

```
69–70
```

```
Before the roll, a group of inimigos working for the campaign’s Vilão attacks
the Herói, intent on destroying as much of the projects source or other resources
as possible.
```

71–72
```

```
Before the roll, a Tempestade moves into the Área that threatens to persist until the
project is completed. The closer to completion the Herói gets on the project, the
more violent the Tempestade becomes. It’s possible that the Tempestade is conscious, or
that someone is controlling the Tempestade to stand in the Herói’s way.
```

d100 Event

73–74

```
After the roll, the Herói falls asleep. They go on to complete the project in their
dreams, but they have no access to that progress while they’re awake. The Herói
can rectify this by finding a way to physically enter into their dreams, where
the completed project can be found.
```

75–76

```
Before the roll, a band of goblins barge in on the Herói. If the Herói has been
fighting goblins on their recent adventures, the goblins attempt to run away
with the Origem do Projeto. Otherwise, the goblins are merely curious about the
project, and the Herói can make dois project rolls if they choose to explain it and
have the goblins help.
```

77–78

```
After the roll, the Herói watches as qualquer progress made is reversed—as if the
project were moving backward through time. qualquer personagem Familiar with
Psiônica recognizes the phenomena as a chrono-anomaly. The project loses
the same amount of progress each successive night until the Herói finds and
stops the source of the anomaly, which restores the project’s progress.
```

79–80

```
Before the roll, the Herói hears a Voz beckoning them into the nearest wode
to work on their project. Each time the Herói makes a Lançamento de Projeto in A Silva,
they make três times the progress but feel more pressure to stay in A Silva
forever.
```

81–82

```
After the roll, the Herói stumbles upon Conhecimento of an expert a day’s travel
away who could complete the project, and who possesses a Origem do Projeto or
Guia for another Herói’s project.
```

83–84

```
Before the roll, Fogo rips through the Herói’s Origem do Projeto or other materials
and threatens to destroy the entire project. If the Herói puts out the Fogo before
everything is lost, they find that the Fogo activated secret notes that double each
subsequent Lançamento de Projeto for the project.
```

85–86

```
After the roll, a Autor NPC approaches the Herói and asks if they would like to
make the project “a little more exciting.” If the Herói agrees, the Autor narrates
the Herói’s progress on the project, prompting another Lançamento de Projeto. If the second
roll is lower than the first, the Herói subtracts the second roll from the original
roll. If it’s equal or higher, the Herói adds the second roll to the original roll.
```

87–88

```
Before the roll, the Herói’s Rival reluctantly comes procurando the Herói’s help on
their own project. If the Herói agrees, the Herói makes their Lançamento de Projeto toward
the Rival’s project, and the Diretor makes the Rival’s Lançamento de Projeto toward the
Herói’s project.
```

10 temporary Vigor.

then in some future Combate, an NPC of the Diretor’s choice turns out to be a
friend or relative of the wagoneer. They leave the battle peacefully when they
recognize the Herói.

After the roll, the Herói suddenly no longer understands or comprehends the

If they leave the project alone for the next dois respites, they’ll be able to
comprehend the research De Novo, gaining an automatic Avanço before the
next Lançamento de Projeto.

to negotiate if the Herói doesn’t approach them aggressively.

99–100
```

Before the roll, an Elemental springs forth from the Origem do Projeto and pulls the
Herói into a duel. If the Herói can survive 3 rounds of Combate with the Elemental
on their own, the Elemental vanishes and leaves behind a completed project.
If the Herói flees, falls Inconsciente, or gets help from an aliado, the Elemental
destroys the Origem do Projeto as they disappear.

**Crafting and Research Events**

Draw Steel

**Go Undercover**

```
Item Pré-requisito: Especial
Origem do Projeto: Nenhuma
Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic: Intuição or Presença
Objetivo de Projeto: 15
Going undercover to spy on a group of people is a cheap and easy way
to find information you’re looking for. Choose an Organização when
you undertake this activity. Completing this project grants you access
to maps, Conhecimento about an Organização’s operations, or some other
piece of Conhecimento that would be considered common or obscure (see
the Discover Lore project).
```

```
At the Diretor’s discretion, you must have a Disfarce, a signet ring,
a Especial tattoo, or some other indication that you belong to the
Organização in Ordem to start this project. Additionally, the Diretor
can decide that the Conhecimento you seek can’t be gained through this
project, but must be sought out by infiltrating the Organização as part
of an adventure.
```

```
Complications
This project has its own Especial complications. The first time you
complete this project for an Organização, you have a 25 percent chance
of being caught. Each time you complete this project De Novo with the
same Organização, the chance of being caught increases by 25 percent
and the Objetivo de Projeto increases by 30. If you are caught while going
undercover, members of the Organização pursue you ruthlessly as the
Diretor determines.
```

```
Additionally, while you work to complete this project, you Músculo be
called upon by the Organização to complete a task you Músculo not want
to do. Falha to complete the task leads to you being caught. You can
avoid the task by fleeing the Organização, but this prevents you from
completing the project and makes it impossible for you to undertake
this project De Novo with the same Organização.
```

```
Downtime Projects
```

**Hone Carreira Skills**

Item Pré-requisito: Nenhuma
Origem do Projeto: Nenhuma
Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic: Intuição
**Objetivo de Projeto:** 240 if your Carreira granted you dois skills, or 360 if your
Carreira granted you três skills

You revisit your previous Vida to freshen up on the experience it
provided you. When this project is complete, you gain an Vantagem on tests
made using the skills provided by your Carreira.

**Learn From a Master**

Item Pré-requisito: Nenhuma
Origem do Projeto: An NPC of a higher Nível, or records of such an NPC’s
teachings in a idioma you know
Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic: Your highest characteristic
**Objetivo de Projeto:** Varies

When you seek to learn from a master, you choose the goal you wish to
work on as well as the Benefício you would gain from it. The Diretor tells
you whether the master or the materials they’ve left behind are able to
teach you what you want to learn.

```
Acquire Habilidade
You gain um signature Habilidade of your choice from the master’s Classe
(gaining a second signature Habilidade if the master is of the same Classe as
you). If the master is a Tático, you can gain the Golpe Now Habilidade
instead. You can’t gain this Benefício De Novo for the same Classe.
```

```
Hone Habilidade
You sharpen the effectiveness of um of your abilities of your choice.
Choose between adding a +1/+1/+1 dano Bônus to the Habilidade, or
improving the Distância of a À Distância Habilidade by 2. An Habilidade can be honed
only once this way.
```

```
Improve Control
You learn to use um of your heroic abilities more efficiently, reducing
its baseline Recurso Heróico cost by 1 (to a minimum of 1). You can gain
this Benefício only once for qualquer Habilidade.
```

```
Hone Carreira Skills Events
d10 Event

intent to remain a Herói gains a Herói token. However, if they do so—or if they Mentir to
say they will return to their old Carreira—the Objetivo de Projeto increases by 50 points as
their old colleague refuses to help them.

is an Artesão or a Sábio depending on the Herói’s Carreira, as the Diretor determines.

```
Recipes
Tipo of Recipe Item Pré-requisito Benefits
Modern Common ingredients (flour, carrots, beef, and so forth) Hearty
```

```
Vintage or home Key ingredients (starfruit, kindleseeds, oarfish, and so forth) Comforting
```

```
Ancient or lost Rare or extinct ingredients (honeylilies, steel apples, and so forth) Sobrenatural Poder
```

```
Learn New idioma
Item Pré-requisito: Nenhuma
Origem do Projeto: Texts or instruction that teaches the idioma you want
to learn
Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic: Razão or Intuição
Objetivo de Projeto: 120
```

```
When you start this project, choose a idioma taught by the project
source. When the project is complete, you understand the idioma.
```

```
Learn New Perícia
Item Pré-requisito: Nenhuma
Origem do Projeto: Texts or instruction that teaches the Perícia you want to
learn
Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic: Razão or Intuição
Objetivo de Projeto: 120
```

```
When you start this project, choose a Perícia taught by the Origem do Projeto.
When the project is complete, you have that Perícia.
```

```
Perfect New Recipe
Item Pré-requisito: Varies
Origem do Projeto: A recipe in a idioma you know, or someone who can
tutor you in that recipe
Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic: Razão or Intuição
Objetivo de Projeto: 100
```

```
When you start this project, you choose a recipe for a specific Tipo of
dish. The Item Pré-requisito for the project is the ingredients required,
which depend on the recipe and which Músculo be difficult to acquire
depending on the recipe and its place of origin. You gain a +3 Bônus to
the Lançamento de Projeto if the recipe is um from your Cultura.
When you complete the project, you can make five servings of food
from the recipe as a Descanso activity whenever you have access to the
ingredients. You and other criaturas taking a Descanso with you can eat a
serving of the food and gain its benefits (see below).
```

```
A criatura who eats a serving of food from a particular Tipo of recipe
gains um of the following benefits, which lasts until the criatura takes
another Descanso.
Comforting: When the criatura fails a Teste de Resistência, they can choose to
succeed instead. This Benefício then ends.
Hearty: The criatura increases their Recoveries by 1 at the end of the
Descanso in which the food is consumed.
Sobrenatural Poder: The criatura temporarily increases um of their
characteristic scores by 1 (to a maximum of 6).
```

```
A criatura can Benefício from the food of only um recipe at a time, and
can’t Benefício from more than um serving of a recipe at a time.
```

Other Projects

Not all heroes want to craft or research during their time between
adventures. Some Músculo wish to build organizations, reconnect with
family or friends, or just go fishing.

**Community Service**

Item Pré-requisito: Nenhuma
Origem do Projeto: Nenhuma
Lançamento de Projeto Characteristic: Varies
**Objetivo de Projeto:** 75

When you start this project, you must be in a settlement or other
location where people gather, and you must be in that same place each
time you make a Lançamento de Projeto for the project. You can undertake several
Community Service projects at the same time, but each um must be in
a different community.

While undertaking this project, you provide help to people in need,
doing odd jobs, tutoring Vida skills, cleaning streets or public spaces,
finding lost valuables, and the like. The Diretor determines the
characteristic that applies to the Lançamento de Projeto based on the activities
you undertake. When you complete this project, you receive a random
Consumível Tesouro of the Diretor’s choice from someone in the
community as thanks for your hard work.

Draw Steel

```
Fishing Events
d10 Event
```

```
1
```

```
While fishing, the Herói reels in a talking peixe. The peixe informs the Herói of
qualquer events that have occurred within 10 squares of the body of Água where
they were caught over the last week, or provides um piece of Forbidden
Conhecimento (see the Discover Lore project), as the Diretor determines.
```

```
2
```

```
While fishing, the Herói reels in a note in a bottle. The note is written in Anjali
and binds the reader into a deal with a powerful Diabo if read out loud. This
gives the Diabo ownership of the reader’s soul in Mercado for rolling an
additional d10 on all future Fishing project rolls.
```

```
3
```

```

Chapter 13
```

# **Deuses e Religião**

rden is a fantasy world in which the gods are objectively real.
In spite of this the people of Orden, regardless of Linhagem, do
not believe the gods control everything that happens in the
world. They believe the gods created a natural world with its own
cycles that are sometimes predictable, but which cannot be
understood. It rained last Lyleth, and the Lyleth before that, so it’ll
probably rain this Lyleth—but maybe not! And if not, that may be
because the gods are displeased. But it Músculo just as easily be because
the gods are bored, or fickle or—even more likely, it has nothing to do
with the gods, and there’s no way to know which.

When a river floods or crops fail, some people may curse the gods, but
those people do not all believe a god caused these events. They may
curse simply because the gods didn’t prevent catastrophe. They do
not think, “Why did the gods do that?” They think, “Why did the gods
make a world that behaves like this?”

The gods are powerful, but forbidden from acting directly upon or
within the world. To enact their will, they use intermediaries—beings
of Semideus-like status, once mortals, who now serve their patron god
in eternity. Many humans call these beings saints, while the other
speaking peoples use the term heroes, or legendary heroes, not to be
confused with the heroes you make using the personagem Criação rules
in this book.

Each god has many saints, some obscure. They sometimes manifest
in the world. These encounters are always brief, Conduzindo sages and
theologians to conclude there must be some limit to how much time
or energy these saints and legendary heroes can Gastar on the prime
Variedade. Who created or enforces these limits?

No um knows.

As a result of this complex tapestry of belief and personalities, a Fazendeiro
in Aendrim Músculo call upon Adûn for strength while tilling the Terra.
But if a cool breeze suddenly came along, easing the Morder of the Sol on
their back, they would almost certainly not thank Adûn or qualquer of his
saints. They would probably thank Saint Elspeth the Blithe, sometimes
called the Summer Breeze. If they had a neighbor or relative with a
shrine to Saint Elspeth in their home, they Músculo give that person a
small gift or offering and ask them to place it on their shrine. More
likely, they would silently promise to do this, and then forget or get
Distraído.

If questioned about this—“Why did you call upon um god, but thank
the saint of a completely different god?”—they would first be Surpreso
by the question. It would not have occurred to them to examine this
behavior. If pressed they would say, “Oh, I’m sure they worked it out
between them.” They would not imagine, “Adûn told Viras, who told
her saint, Elspeth, to send a cooling breeze,” but they would assume

```
something like that happened and not worry overmuch about the
details. They called out, they received aid—that’s what’s important.
```

If no aid is forthcoming folks assume this is because the gods and saints
are all very busy and cannot be arsed to answer every Prece. People
are never Surpreso when the gods and saints are silent. They are
usually silent.

Churches and Temples
Most religions in Orden organize themselves into hierarchies and build
temples or cathedrals, but some religions are little more than traditions
handed down from shaman to shaman, or wise-woman to wise-daugh-
ter. Some religions are secret!

Because the gods are forbidden from acting directly upon the world,
churches and temples in Orden are consecrated to saints, or heroes.
There are no temples to Ord or churches of Cavall. Instead, there is the
Church of Zarok the Law-Giver and the Church of Saint Llewellyn the
Valiant. Everyone knows which god these heroes and saints serve, it’s
common Conhecimento. A Humano in Vasloria Músculo call out to Cavall for
aid in times of need but they know that, should Cavall choose to help,
it will be by sending um of his saints.
The most popular saints and heroes can have several churches—
meaning distinct organizations—devoted to them, each with their own
rituals. In Corwell, there is the Church of Saint Llewellyn the Valiant,
but there is also the smaller Church of Saint Llewellyn the Charitable
with only a few temples.

Usually, these churches recognize each other as expressing different,
equally valid teachings of the same saint, but occasionally churches
compete to see which among them is the “true” church. The saints
don’t discourage this, so they must, in some sense, approve.
There are churches dedicated to Natureza or Conhecimento or the Sol, with
no Tempo Limpo moral or ethical component to them. There are evil churches,
churches devoted to dark saints and tyrant gods. But the saints and
heroes listed here each have churches that, however esoteric their
teachings (usually referred to as the “speech” or “words” of the saint
or Herói) expect their clergy to go forth into the world and perform
good deeds—tend to the sick, ease pain, perform birth, Morte, and
union rituals. These churches all have Acólitos and abbots, censors
and conduits. It is not so much that Grole the um-Handed was, in
Vida, principally concerned with the spiritual wellbeing of his people ,
but rather that this is what people expect of churches. So, as a Religião
grows, it soon conforms to the expectations of the people such that
even the church of Khorvath Who Slew A Thousand has conduits who
Curar the sick and tend to the souls of their people.

Interspecies Worship
Elves, dwarves, and orcs revere their own creator gods. Val, Ord, and Kul
respectively. Humans, uniquely, worship many gods. The difference
between the Incontáveis Deuses Jovens of the humans and the Elder
Gods who created the other speaking peoples is not well understood.

```
Dwarves mostly venerate Anão heroes, humans mostly worship
Humano saints, and so on ... But this is just a side Efeito of the fact that
members of the same Linhagem share the same Cultura and idioma
and Personagem-assemble along those lines. qualquer sufficiently large city,
regardless of which species founded it, has churches and temples
to gods of many species because cities attract people of many
different species.
Each Cultura’s pantheon reflects the mores and folkways of the people
who live there. In far northern Vanigar, villains in folktales often gain
their Poder by tricking others through clever wordplay. Riddles.
Though they are villains, they are clever, and this earns them some
respect even from their inimigos. So the Vanigar pantheon includes
Holkatya, a trickster god.
```

```
Whereas Vasloria has no folk tradition of trickster figures, and so has no
trickster god. Instead, villains in Vasloriano folktales tend to be people
who seek quick ways to Poder in Ordem to avoid honest work. So
Vasloria has the dark god Cyrvis who teaches that Magia can subvert
Destino and make you master of not only your destiny, but also the world.
This also reveals the common Vasloriano’s Atitude toward Magia.
The gods of each pantheon tell you what the people of that region
value, and what they fear, disapprove of, or distrust. The Vasloriano
pantheon is wholly different from the pantheon of Vanigar which is
different from the pantheon of Rioja. The gods and saints can hear their
Adoradores anywhere in the timescape and even small cities can have
```

```
temples to distant gods of other peoples and regions. All it takes is um
dedicated Conduíta to establish a church of their saint or Herói in some
distant land.
```

```
For instance, A Alta Cidade de Dalrath, a small barony in northern
Aendrim, has a temple to Sektahre the Boatman, a saint of Khemhara, a
distant desert region. The people of Dalrath do not find this strange. The
priestess of Sektahre does all the same things qualquer native curate would
do: perform rituals, Curar the sick, and otherwise tend to the spiritual
and physical wellbeing of the locals without asking much in return.
Some people may be Desconfiado of a stranger peddling their Religião
far from home, but yet more people consider the Presença of such a
priestess a sign that their city must be very important indeed.
Because of all these gods and saints, Religião in Orden is a very à la carte
affair. There are Humano heroes in the elf pantheon. There are Anão
saints in many Humano pantheons. Elder or younger, the gods do not
care much about their followers’ biology. If you devote your Vida to the
teachings of a god and do good works in their name, you can expect to
be rewarded regardless of your Linhagem. And, though the Era dos Santos
is long past, most folk believe it is still possible for a mortal to ascend to
sainthood or herodom, even in this late age.
```

```
Lastly, though rulers across the land instinctively believe the gods are
paying more attention to them because they are queens or dukes or
the heads of a powerful wizard Ordem or guild ... there is no evidence
of this. As far as theologists can tell, the gods seem to view every soul
as equally worthy. Many of the Contos de Santos e Heróis Recurso
characters of enormous Poder Divino battling over the soul of a normal
person with no station or Poder or inheritance.
As much as it annoys the great and the good, the gods view all
mortals as equals.
```

Evil Gods and Saints

```
The gods and saints presented in this chapter are popular and
well-known. Their priests, shamans, or god-callers serve the public weal
and tend to the souls of the people.
But the world is not for heroes alone. There are villains, as well as those
who are simply misguided or desperate. Every pantheon has saints,
even gods, who teach the virtues of selfishness, cruelty, the pursuit of
Poder for its own sake, and the right of the Forte to do as they please.
```

```
These religions do not usually build public temples and worship in
the Receptivo, but most communities know, or very strongly suspect, who
among them serve evil gods and saints.
Among the people of Vasloria, there are the gods Nikros, o Tirano and
Cyrvis o Lich, evil gods, each with their own saints. When tyrants
rule, these religions tend to come out from the basements and sew-
er-temples and start worshipping openly.
```

Afterlife in Orden

```
Folk in Orden believe that most, maybe all, living things have a soul,
which is the source of personality, creativity, and memory. The loss of
um’s soul, either through bargaining with a Diabo, or being consumed
by a Demônio or otherwise trapped by a warlock, results in slowly losing
your personality, your distinctiveness—even memory.
However, there is no popular idea that everyone’s soul is immortal and
persists forever after Morte. Most people believe their soul dissipates
after Morte and becomes um with Criação. When asked where the
soul goes after Morte, the elf Sábio responded by blowing out a candle
and asking, “Where did the Fogo go?”
```

```
How To Use This Chapter
Draw Steel isn’t about Religião qualquer more than it is about
idioma or Tesouro, but understanding how Religião works in
a day-to-day sense can help make the game world feel more
real. The people in Orden aren’t qualquer more religious than the
people of Terra were in the premodern era. It is a factor in their
lives, but not the only factor—and for some people, not a very
important um.
Obviously, Conduíta and Censurador jogadores can use this chapter
to choose a saint, each saint’s entry also lists which domains
they represent. But each god also has a list of domains, so
an enterprising jogador could just invent a new saint, Herói, or
Arauto choosing dois domains from a god’s list.
But qualquer jogador Músculo wonder, “Does my personagem follow the
teachings of qualquer saint or god?” Think about the people you
know in the real world who wear religious or quasi-religious
talismans every day. A symbol on a necklace, a sticker on their
car, a tattoo. Normal people often carry religious talismans,
your personagem in Draw Steel Músculo not be particularly religious,
but they Músculo still carry a religious talisman just because it’s
a family tradition or to remind themselves of the religious
instruction they received in church as a child.
We wrote a lot of words in this chapter because we wanted to
give characters from all ancestries a few choices when it comes
to saints and heroes. But your personagem can ignore all of this if
you think Religião isn’t a big part of their Vida.
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

In some cultures, exceptions are made for those mortals who lived an
especially virtuous Vida.

Much the same way the humans of Vanigar believe the bravest among
them live on after Morte drinking and telling tales at the Mesa de Guerra—the
wartable—most elves believe that should they live a Vida of sufficient
meaning, should they do great deeds and embody Val’s ethos, they
earn the right to join Val in Arcádia after Morte. There they will live in a
timeless faerie world, “the world that should have been.”

Most dwarves believe that those members of each generation who best
distinguish themselves earn the right to live forever in Ord’s memory.
This, they believe, is where their heroes go after Morte. Uniquely among
the speaking peoples, the dwarves believe their god is watching them,
watching the world. Ord cannot act, but he judges and remembers.

Some people in Orden, like the Hakaan and the orcs believe their
ancestors watch over them, although there is no agreement whether
their ancestor’s souls are watching over them, or just their memory.
Or something in between. Sages differ. This belief among the orcs and
Hakaan is more of an Atitude, an assumption, than a Religião.

Conduits and Censors

“Conduíta” and “Censurador” are not a titles within qualquer church—they are jobs
or ranks. An abbot, rector, even a bishop may be, or may have been, a
Conduíta or a Censurador. Conduits and censors are those members of the
church expected to go out into the world and actively, sometimes very
actively, represent their saint’s ethos. It is for this purpose conduits and
censors are given access to powerful prayers.

qualquer sufficiently large Organização has conduits and censors just like
they have shadows and wizards. The thieves’ guild needs healers, just as
the church needs spies! A Conduíta who works for the thieves’ guild still
serves their saint which implicitly means the church approves of the
guild’s activities and the dois organizations are at least pointing in the
same Direção if not actively allied.

Churches have bureaucracy just like qualquer Organização and while some
prelates, abbots, bishops, or hierarchs are conduits, many are not. They
are normal people who serve the church in administrative, political,
or Burocrática roles. While they know the same minor orisons every
Acólito and abbot know, they do not go out into the world righting
wrongs, and so do not gain access to the powers of the Conduíta or Censurador.

The prayers Acólitos perform in churches are little more than magical
rituals. They say the right words, make the right gestures, touch the
appropriate fetish or talisman, and wounds close, curses are lifted,
blessings bestowed. There’s no direct connection in these examples
between the Acólito and their god or saint. Though, even a lowly
Acólito can expect to find their prayers fall on deaf ears if they fail to
uphold the tenets of their faith.

Should the Acólito continue in their studies and deeds and earn the
rank of Conduíta or Censurador, they gain access to greater prayers granted
them by their saint. As they Avançar in their faith they call upon their
saint more directly, and they begin to form a personal relationship with
their saint. It is a feeling that develops whereby the Conduíta learns the ...
mood, for lack of a better term, of their saint or Herói.

As they gain experience, a Conduíta or Censurador may even enter into
dialogue with their saint. When they call upon their saint for Poder in
battle, their saint personally answers them. They Músculo literally be on
first-name terms. At even higher levels, conduits begin to get a sense
of the greater Poder behind the saint or legendary Herói: their god,
who begins answering prayers directly. They become, in Efeito, little
mini-saints. The pathway from high-Nível Conduíta or Censurador to saint is
now obscure, but was once well-known. In earlier ages of the world, it

```
was expected that certain Sagrado heroes who had served their god and
saint well would—should appropriately dramatic circumstances reveal
themselves—be elevated to sainthood.
The Deities and Domains table and the Saints and Domains table
summarize each of the gods and saints mentioned in this chapter and
their available domains.
```

```

Draw Steel

```
Va l
Domains: Criação, Conhecimento, Vida, Natureza, Proteção
```

```
Val, the Nobre Lord, First Among Equals, is the patron of the elves.
He created the celestials—the elvos verdadeiros, second of the five speaking
peoples—who then created the younger elves: the high, wode, and
Sombra elves. His name is the root of the Caeliano word “valiant,”
and the dwarves named the most precious ore in Orden—Valiar, the
truemetal—after him.
Val holds that the greatest purpose a thinking being can commit
themselves to is the Criação of art and the appreciation of beauty. He
keeps the magical, elf-haunted forests called wodes close to his heart
because they represent his Visão for Orden. What the world could
have been. His growing disgust with the concept of Guerra led him to leave
Orden and take up residence in his private Variedade, Arcádia where all
elves hope to someday join their patron.
```

**Heroes of the Elves**

```
The legendary heroes of the elves are once-mortal heroes who now
dwell in Arcádia and make up Val’s court there. They answer prayers
and dispense blessings and boons, even manifest in the world during
times of great need. (Though, like all the speaking people’s saints and
heroes, what these legendary figures consider “great need” is very
personal and has little to do with politics or great kingdoms.)
The Alto Elfo heroes detailed in this book are A Sea of Suns, the Provar of
Morning, and Ripples of Honey on a Shore of Gold. The Elfo Silvestre heroes
are Yllin Dyrvis, Thyll Hylacae, and Illwyv li Orchiax.
```

```
A Sea of Suns
Domains: Criação, Vida
```

```
A Sea of Suns, also known as the Composer.
Credited with inventing harmony, it is said that after she discovered
the Poder of blending many voices into um, the elves sang for an entire
century uninterrupted 1. The harmonics so complicated they created
new beings like faeries, dryads, and the elgenwights.
```

```
The Composer discovered, or invented, the Poder of Música to
manipulate reality. Her troubadours, it was said, could return the dead
to Vida. “In the Música, you can live forever.” Legend has it she was at the
battle of Kalas Valiar when the first Exército da Noite besieged its walls.
When their Corrupção engines Enfraquecido the impenetrable walls,
she stood alone on the parapets and sang. For forty days did her Voz
bolster the walls, stemming the flood of evil. Her song ended only when
her Vida was taken by Um Coração Preso em Âmbar, the sorcerer-Assassino of
the star elves.
```

```
1 If this story wasn’t invented by the dwarves or humans, it must at least
have passed through um of their cultures. The celestials did not reckon time
the way younger species do and would not have said “for an entire century.”
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

The Provar of Morning
**Domains:** Criação, Conhecimento

The Provar of Morning, also known as the Librarian.

Credited with building the first library, most scholars consider this a
real, historical event (never a certainty with the tales of the legendary
heroes) and adventurers through all ages have sought this legendary
building. If, indeed, it was a building.

He canonized the idea that Conhecimento, truth, was a kind of beauty. The
Library of Morning was a temple to thought, wisdom, scholarship. It
contained plays, poems, histories, treatises on the Natureza of reality. The
Conhecimento held within was incalculable. Legends say it held codices
written by the elder dragons, though modern scholars suspect this is
a literary conceit, as there is no evidence the elder dragons bothered
with writing.

Ripples of Honey on a Shore of Gold
**Domains:** Vida, Proteção

Ripples of Honey on a Shore of Gold, also known as Warkiller, the
Diplomat, was both scholar, Sábio, and Soldado. She served as emissary
between the humans and the dragons when the former sought Guerra
against the latter. For many years she brokered Paz, but she could not
stem the tides of Guerra forever.

In the end, her efforts failed, and the elder dragons live no more in
this world. Like Val, the Diplomat hated Guerra so much, after her Falha
she sought to pen a new codex. A work so powerful it would bind the
world. The Codex Pax Universalis would Banir the concept of Guerra
from Orden. Alas, in the end she realized there was only um way to
finish her great work, and she was not willing to take that final step.

Yllin Dyrvis
**Domains:** Conhecimento, Natureza

Yllin Dyrvis, also known as the Fera Heart, the Wodespeaker, the
Guardião, witnessed the Composer’s first song, and took it upon
themselves to communicate with and care for the speaking criaturas
A Sea of Suns created. The dryads, elgenwights, the Gigante birds and
intelligent peixe who populated the ancient wode that once covered
all Orden, all came under the Fera Heart’s care. Dyrvis learned their
speech and taught them who they were.

To this day, many ages of the world later, A Silva elves consider
themselves the stewards of the speaking criaturas, and those criaturas
rely upon A Silva elves for Proteção.

Thyll Hylacae
**Domains:** Vida, Natureza

Thyll Hylacae, the Forestal, Apothachron, also known as the Sacrifício.
Thyll spoke to the plants, learned their truths—discovered many
magics Escondida within. The Poder to Curar, harm, change. It was Hylacae
who first sensed, then learned, the idioma of trees. She studied, cared
for them, and protected them when the folk of farm and field came to
cut them down.

Though she was mighty in warlore, she could not be everywhere. In the
end, she sacrificed herself for the trees, the ritual she performed uplifted
a small population of trees, creating the derwic—the thinking speaking
tree-peoples few of whom remain in Orden.

```
Illwyv li Orchiax
Domains: Natureza, Proteção
Illwyv li Orchiax, the Moonknight, Marshall of the Gloaming,
Manslayer. When humans first arrived in Orden—it is said—they were
welcomed by the other speaking peoples. But they were unlike the
other creations in the world. While the dwarves cut rock for the ore
within, humans cut down trees simply because they were in the way.
Other ancestries had their own territories and homelands, but humans
sought constant expansion into even the most inhospitable territories.
```

```
Illwyv it was who first realized the folly of treating with these criaturas. A
great Caçador of the Corte do Carvalho, she gathered her band of Elite Helriath
Harriers and made Guerra on the humans who would kill A Silva.
```

```
Ord
Domains: Criação, Conhecimento, Proteção, Sol, Guerra
```

```
Ord, the Maker, the Engineer, is the patron of the dwarves. Ord, along
with his siblings Aan, Eth, and Kul, created Orden. These four saw the
world as a dynamic expression of their philosophies.
Ord values integrity, honor, faithfulness to an ideal. Courage in
battle and fair play. Treating your opponent honorably, Ord teaches,
is an expression of your own worthiness. Ord is associated with
permanence, which some elder dwarves take to mean a kind of slavish
devotion to tradition. But Ord teaches permanence is the quality of
reliability, of steadfastness. Young dwarves who chafe at the stale and
stifling traditions of their elders remind the greybeards that Ord is the
Maker. He expects his children to create marvels, to bring forth new
discoveries, new insights. To remake the world anew each generation.
```

**Heroes of the Dwarves**

```
The following heroes are venerated by many dwarves and others
who follow Ord.
```

```
Zarok the Law-Giver
Domains: Proteção, Guerra
Zarok the Law-Giver. Zarok the Professor. Zarok who is Justiça.
```

```
The first, great Herói of the dwarves, Zarok was a noted general,
diplomat, and poet. In his time each Anão city-state had its own laws
which were mostly just lists of offenses with punishments listed next
to them. There was no consistency from um city to another and no
underlying theory of law. The Forte ruled, the rest obeyed.
It was after Zarok retired from his Carreira as a Mestre de Guerra and became
the ambassador to the elves that he undertook a study of how different
cultures express the idea of Justiça. He surveyed the various traditions
of elves, humans, and orcs and wrote The As Conversas —a series of
fictional dialogues in which dois characters, deliberately chosen from
Anão theater so as to be Familiar to his audience, debate the question:
“What are the characteristics of a just Sociedade?”
```

```
The As Conversas marks the beginning of legal theory in Orden. It
sought not only to state what a just Sociedade was, but to prove it ethically
through a series of logical statements. Most of the work concerns itself
with the proper, ethical uses of political Poder. The adversarial system
of legal representation is his.
Zarok teaches that all people should be equal under the law. His is the
principle of fair play—sportsmanship. Respect for your adversary. The
responsibility of the Forte to protect the Fraca.
```

```
Zarok’s The As Conversas are still quoted today. There is a long legal
tradition, when a prestigious lawyer in Capital wishes to write an
amicus brief without revealing their identity, they sign it “Z.”
```

Draw Steel

```
Valak-koth the Seeker
Domains: Conhecimento, Sol
Valak-koth the Seeker, the Delver, the Fogo Inextinguível, Koth Who
Brought Luz to Darkness, said she heard voices in the rock as a child.
These days this would result in a visit to the apothecary or a change
in diet, but in those days the world was young and a child who heard
voices Músculo Turno out to be a prophet of Ord. Her parents listened and
soon Nenhuma doubted.
```

```
She would run, heedless of danger, into the dark caves below and
wherever she pointed, marvels were found: metals, gems, fantastic ores.
Caves as big as nations. It was Valak-koth it was who first discovered
Aerithyst, a Gema Solar, a crystal mineral which glows upon contact with
living things.
Valak-koth teaches bravery in the face of the unknown, the Virtude of
curiosity, to seek endlessly and quest for Conhecimento, not to fear the
darkness. To bring Luz into dark places. Valak-koth it was who first
discovered O Mundo Inferior, A Escuridão Abaixo de Tudo, though it was not
recognized as a separate Variedade until after her Morte. After her Morte,
the original Sungem she found refused to dim. It was enshrined in
her temple-tomb, now lost along with the ancient Pedra Anão city of
Kas Koriar.
```

```
Stakros the Engineer
Domains: Criação, Conhecimento
```

```
Stakros o Engenheiro, a Mente Máquina, o Operador, founder of the
Ordem da Fabricação.
Stakros it was— not a steel Anão—who forged the first strife-engine,
a great Guerra-walker manned by thirty dwarves. At the battle of Kalas
Mithral, the Guerra-walker grappled with the legion of yllindyr the star
elves summoned to defeat the walls of the steel Anão capital.
```

```
After the Guerra, Stakros turned his talents to peaceful pursuits. He forged
the first Mergulhador de Magma, designed to withstand enormous temperatures
and pressures, all the while protecting the Operador within. Inside
his marvel Stakros personally dove into the great volcano Oxor-myr,
returning with marvelous ores never before seen in Orden. His
design soon evolved into a variety of armored frames to suit a variety
of purposes.
Stakros teaches the value of Conhecimento for Conhecimento’s sake, and the
Poder of the mind to overcome qualquer obstacle. He also teaches that
Conhecimento is Poder, and in unready hands can only be dangerous.
```

Kul

```
Domains: Conhecimento, Vida, Sol, Trapaça, Guerra
Kul, Father of Flames, Lord of the Forge, the Cleansing Fogo who put Fogo
and magma within the world at its Criação.
```

```
He saw his sibling gods creating their own children and placing them
within the world, and so followed suit, creating the orcs, the last of the
original Cinco Povos Falantes.
Kul’s Fogo is the Fogo that destroys, but it is also the Fogo that creates,
the Fogo of the forge, the Fogo that makes meat safe to eat, the Fogo that
cauterizes wounds. Kul teaches that action is the defining characteristic
of being. Kul’s heroes are not philosophers or poets, but warriors
and hunters.
```

```
Uniquely among the Elder Creator Gods, Kul does not desire worship—
finds it distasteful. Orcs still call out to Kul in desperate times as “Kul
Who Once Spoke.” But in those moments, they do not call out for
aid—only that Kul witness them, and that they Músculo prove worthy of
his attention.
```

```
Heroes of the Orcs
The following heroes are venerated by many orcs and others
who follow Kul.
```

```
Khorvath Who Slew a Thousand
Domains: Sol, Guerra
```

```
When Khorvath, Líder de Guerra for the Elétrico orc clan set out with her
warband of bloodrunners, they numbered less than fifty. When they
finally arrived at the Cidade Solar, seat of the pharaoh of Khemhara, they
had grown to over dois thousand orcs from over thirty orc clans, all
eager for battle. Legends later swelled that number to ten thousand. 
Upon their arrival, the bloodrunners found their prospective employer
embattled and surrounded by inimigos, the pharaoh’s brother having
raised rebellion against him. Principally due to Khorvath’s help, the
pharaoh’s brother was killed and his army defeated. But the pharaoh
died in the battle, and Khorvath found herself and her warband
without a patron in an alien land surrounded by inimigos fighting a Guerra
of succession.
```

```
“What do we do, Líder de Guerra?” Her Capitão da Morte asked. 
Khorvath oriented herself and pointed northwest. “Home is that
way. We march!”
```

```
Capitão da Morte Voyrik’s eyes went wide. “It’s três thousand miles,” he
pointed out—and the journey to Khemhara had not been uneventful!
“Best get started,” Khorvath said, and set off. 
```

```
How long it took the bloodrunners of the Elétrico to cross the desert
is not well-attested. It took four or six months depending on which
accounts you read, but even six months would make their march a
legendary journey.
Opposed at every Turno by the local Nobre houses and then eventually
the desert clans who sought the bounty placed on Khorvath’s head, the
ten thousand grew in battle prowess as they demolished qualquer inimigo
foolish enough to get in their way. Given the many tens of thousands
of warriors the bloodrunners dispatched over the course of four (or six)
months, it may well be that Khorvath’s sobriquet was literal.
```

```
Sucesso was a double edged sword. The more victories they earned
in battle, the easier they were to follow. “Our inimigos Andar the red
road,” Voyrik once said, looking at the vast swath of blood they left in
their wake.  
“We have nothing to fear,” Khorvath said. “These people fight for
pride, or a bounty. We’re fighting for our lives. All it takes is um good
punch in the nose and they retreat.” And indeed this proved true
for many weeks.
```

```
Eventually três of the desert tribes allied themselves and this was a
coalition that could take a few bloody noses without giving up. They
cornered the bloodrunners in a ravine that led to a Montanha pass. It
was possible to Navegação the narrow pass, but only dois or três orcs
at a time. It would take hours to retreat that way. And the três tribes
blocked their way out.
Khorvath saw the way. She unwound her mother’s hand wraps from
her forearms and wrapped them around her own fists. The brown
stains on the knuckles made Khorvath proud.
```

```
“I will take the best Guerreiro from each of the 30 tribes,” Khorvath
pronounced, and word spread almost instantly. Within minutes, the
thirty best warriors among the ten thousand stood with Khorvath. “We
thirty will hold the pass.”
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

Capitão da Morte Voyrik, eyes wide, whispered Khorvath’s name.

Khorvath removed her torque of leadership and handed it to Voyrik.
“When you arrive home, give this to my son.” She looked at the torque
in Voyrik’s hands. “Tell him my last thoughts were of him. And that it is
my wish that this torque inspire him to great deeds.”

The tale of Khorvath’s Thirty is still popular among the orcs, though
everyone listening understands the “três days of Guerra” is pure fiction,
as Nenhuma of the thirty survived. It is nonetheless broadly taken as true.

Khorvath’s Thirty bought the bloodrunners the time they needed to
escape through the pass, and onward Desimpedido.

By the time they reached the eastern side of the Myr, Khorvath’s name
was already a legend, and many bloodrunners wore her clan fetish as
their talisman. Scaling the slopes of the Myr was not easy but as the
orcs descended down the western face, through the clouds, and saw the
endless sea of Verde that was the Great Wode, they cried out together
“Cekana! Cekana!” _The trees! The trees!_

The ten thousand were not home, but they were home free. For this
was territory held by their aliados. The church of Khorvath Who Slew a
Thousand spread quickly and now all orcs invoke her name whenever
faced with a seemingly impossible task.

Khorvath, like most orc heroes, teaches the Virtude of Resiliência. That
great problems are often just many tiny problems in Disfarce and that
by fighting each day as it comes, great battles can be won.

Khorvath Who Slew a Thousand would probably prefer to be
remembered as she was in Vida—Khorvath Who Brought Ten Thousand
Home, but even as um of the chief orc heroes, she has little influence
over the way the people choose to remember her.

Voyrik gave his Líder de Guerra’s torque to her son, who grew to Liderar the
Elétrico first as Líder de Guerra, then chieftain. He was a good ruler for
the Elétrico.

Grole the um-Handed
**Domains:** Vida, Guerra

Grole Uma Mão, Grole que Matou o Santo dos Crânios, lost his left
hand at Batalha de Dur Mothe where he stood alone against the Horda
of deathless and their master, the living saint Morath of Many Tendrils.
Grole thought to buy time for his army to escape the flood of Morte, but
when they saw their Líder de Guerra grappling alone with the Saint of Podridão,
they reversed their retreat. When Morath lashed out with his greataxe
Eviscerador and severed Grole’s left hand from his arm, Grole’s army
surged forward, breaking the tide of deathless.

His army watched as Kul’s Luz descended on their wounded Líder,
and they knew Grole had been chosen by Kul in that moment. At the
last, Grole and Morath fought as equals. Orc Herói and dark Humano saint
grappled atop the ancient hill. With his um good hand Grole plunged
the Fogo Verde, his grandmother’s saber, into Morath’s heart, ending the
Saint of Many Tendrils.

Grole teaches the extraordinary deeds common people can accomplish
if they cast fear from their minds. It was Grole who said, “Even should
an orc be pierced by many arrows, they should still be able to perform
um last act of revenge.”

Grole is the orcish Herói of those facing impossible decisions. He is
favored by most orcish leaders. Grole teaches that, even alone, even
against impossible odds, extraordinary victories are possible. Censors of
Grole often dip their left hand in ink before battle to symbolize Grole’s
missing hand.

```
Khravila Who Ran Forty Leagues
Domains: Conhecimento, Trapaça
Khravila Who Ran Forty Leagues, The Eternal Mensageiro, Khravila The
Implacável.
```

```
On the eve of a Guerra between elves and humans that would certainly
result in the Morte of many orcs caught between the dois great powers,
Khravila’s Morrendo father had been incapable of deciding what should
be done. Equally incapable of choosing who should succeed him as
chieftain—his son or daughter.
At the moment of his Morte, when the god-caller rang the bell of souls
officially announcing her father’s passing to the tribe, Khravila looked
at her brother and saw hesitation. Khravila had never known Dúvida.
```

```
She snatched her tribe’s oriflamme from her father’s dead hands ... and
ran. For many leagues she ran and the tales of the criaturas—manticores,
griffins, chimeras—who barred her passage passed into legend. Orc
children still delight at the tricks and wordplay Khravila employed to
thwart the beasts, avoid fighting, and continue her Épico run.
Less than five hours after her father died, Khravila arrived at the
Corte de Astragalus, forty leagues from home and while many elements of
her legend are certainly mythical, the time and Distância are well attested.
Khravila held forth the oriflamme and announced that, should the elves
continue their assault on the humans, there would be Guerra between them
and her tribe. “Chose quickly,” she said. “My people are right behind me,
and eager for battle.” They could not have known she was bluffing.
```

```
The elves called off their attacks and Khravila brokered Paz between
them and the humans. When her brother arrived with their kin folk
some hours later—itself an impressive feat—Khravila handed him the
oriflamme, and collapsed, dead. It was Khravila the chieftain who ran. It
was Khravila the Implacável who died, a legendary orc Herói.
Khravila teaches the Virtude of persistence, Resiliência, and—above all—
wits. Not only the wits necessary to Contraponto the tests that barred her way,
but to conceive her legendary plan in the first place, and the dedication
to Puxar it off. “Perhaps another orc could have run,” her brother said.
“But only Khravila could have bluffed.”
```

Heroes of the Hakaan

```
Most Hakaan in Orden are animists. They know and respect the four
Deuses Anciões who created the world and believe these gods watch the
world and see what happens within it. But the Hakaan do not create
churches or formal belief systems around this Atitude.
Instead they believe the world is filled with innumerable Natureza spirits.
Each river, tree, Pedra, has their own spirit, which the Hakaan revere.
They have no organized Religião in the way the other ancestries in this
chapter do, though a Hakaan brought up in a city, or among another
people, would naturally venerate in whatever gods and saints are
worshiped by the folk who raised them.
```

```
The Hakaan know they are descended from Pedra giants, but they do
not think of themselves as Pedra giants. They know their ancestors
were tricked by Holkatya, um of the gods of Vanigar, into trading
some of their great strength for the Presságio de Ruína. But while they respect
Holkatya, they do not worship her. Nor do they resent her. She’s merely
a detail of their História.
Hakaan conduits and censors venerate Hakaan heroes who, after doing
great deeds in Vida, were chosen by the gods to take their place among
the stars, becoming constellations. They see the stars at night as a
complex map of legendary Hakaan heroes, and their own ancestors
who watch from above.
```

Draw Steel

```
Mahsiti a Tecelã
Domains: Criação, Conhecimento, Trapaça
```

```
Mahsiti a Tecelã was a fresco painter and mathematician of the
Hakaan who discovered, or invented, a way of drawing very precise
geometric shapes following patterns that repeat at qualquer scale. Believing
it could be a new way to devise spells, she took to weaving tapestries
using lines of thread to better understand the numerical relationships
within the patterns.
It took time to master weaving, but she took to it quickly and produced
a series of essays, each a tapestry, proving correct her suspicions. The
Tapeçarias de Mahsiti are a series of thirteen legendary artifacts of
varying sizes, um as small as a napkin, um over dois hundred feet long.
Each has a powerful spell written into it, available for use by anyone
who can read the patterns.
```

```
um of Mahsiti’s weavings, titled The Pastor e as Ovelhas , was used
by her whole clan when Guerra came to them. The Hakaan had no Dúvida
they could Defensor their home but were equally certain there would
be enormous loss of Vida. Mahsiti suggested they use the tapestry, but
the people of her clan did not understand. Use it how? It was simply a
picture of a tree in a field with many sheep gathered around it.
But this image, as Mahsiti showed, was formed out of thousands of
Repetidor geometric patterns. The tapestry had been a gift from Mahsiti
to her chieftain who hung it in their great receiving hall. Mahsiti cast
the spell within the tapestry—and walked into the tapestry. The people
were amazed and followed.
```

```
When the inimigo army arrived, they found the clan’s villages empty,
and did not notice the tapestry with hundreds of Hakaan depicted
within. Once the inimigo left, Mahsiti finished the spell, and her people
emerged, safe.
Mahsiti teaches that art and science, creativity and Conhecimento, are
the same thing. Those who follow her teachings believe that the act of
creating, of bringing a new idea or work of art into being, is the act of
participating in the same process the gods used to create the world.
```

**Prexaspes the Stargazer**

```
Domains: Natureza, Proteção, Sol
Prexaspes o Observador de Estrelas, o Astrônomo, o Sábio Solar mapped the skies
and was um of the first people in all Orden to correctly calculate the
Repetidor pattern of Orden’s três moons. Because of his growing
mastery of the cycles of Natureza, he predicted a coming famine
and prepared his clan. When the famine came but the people had
storehouses of food ready, he became a Herói of his tribe.
```

```
After receiving the Presságio de Ruína, Prexaspes turned his attention to the
Sol itself. He studied ancient tomes written by scholars of many
people, believing eclipses were predictable events. His research yielded
a pattern, but his Discernimento led him further. What if, he wondered, an
Eclipse was more than a celestial event? What if it was an opening, a
portal? Prexaspes studied the stars and prepared a ritual.
Years later, Prexaspes’ tribe was besieged by hobgoblins and all hope
was lost. He begged his chieftain to continue fighting—not abandon
their homes. The Astronomer promised an Eclipse, and though Nenhuma
doubted his calculations, no um could guess how this could help the
beleaguered and besieged people.
```

```
But the Hakaan trusted their Sábio, and kept up the fight. When
the Eclipse came, Prexaspes performed his experimental ritual
opening a portal to the Sol. A Linha of golden Fogo erupted from the
```

```
portal, evaporating many hobgoblins, but this was just a side-Efeito
of the ritual.
```

```
With his people watching, shielding their eyes from the brilliant Luz,
Prexaspes entered the portal, and emerged on the surface of the Sol. In
that moment, the people knew this was his Ruína. He was only gone a
few moments, but when he emerged from the portal his flesh was solid
sunstuff, and he waded into the remaining battalions of hobgoblins,
destroying them with rays of heat and purifying flame.
Though he died in the act, Prexaspes saved his people becoming a Herói
of all Hakaan, taking his place among the stars as a new constellation.
```

```
Prexaspes teaches that Natureza is a moral good and is worth defending,
and that the Sol is the source of Poder for all Vida on Orden.
```

```
Atossa the Shepherd
Domains: Destino, Proteção, Trapaça
```

```
The great dam built by their ancestors that created Lake Tospah was
going to fail, Atossa’s Presságio de Ruína said. The people would not listen, they
said she read the signs wrong.
When the rains came and would not stop, and the Água in Lake Tospah
rose putting more pressure on the dam, Atossa opened the gates to the
sheep pen and let the tribe’s herd of sheep out.
```

```
The people ran after them, effectively evacuating the village. But the
rains stopped, and the damn did not Explosão. The people returned to their
homes, put the sheep back in the pen, and blamed the shepherd for
worrying too much and Conduzindo them on wild goose chases.
The next year, the rains came De Novo. And this time the lake was already
near capacity. When the shepherd tried to warn the people, they
reminded her that it had rained the year before and there was no
danger—and so would not listen.
```

```
When the first cracks appeared at the base of the dam, Atossa knew her
Feitiço was before her. She took a piece of the broken dam back to the
village to show the elders. They frowned and wondered what Atossa
was up to now, but agreed amongst themselves to go up the valley and
inspect the dam in person.
Atossa tried to warn them they were walking to their Ruína, and
became even more agitated when the rest of the village followed. When
the elders reached the cracked dam, they sounded no alarm. Instead,
they argued and debated, “Chewing their beards”— rish javid —the
Hakaan say about elders who argue instead of acting.
```

```
Desperate, Atossa climbed to the top of the dam, and dove into the
Água, Nadador down to the bottom of the lake where she could see
the Pedra cracking. Her people were on the other side.
When the crack widened and Água began to pour through at
incredible pressure, the people panicked and ran. But Atossa was not
worried. This was her Ruína. She knew what to do.
```

```
She let the flowing Água carry her toward the widening crack until her
body slammed against the Pedra, Posicionamento de Palco the Água. The Hakaan are
famed for being able to hold their Sopro, but though her people ran as
quickly as they could, there was no way Atossa could block the Água
long enough.
When the dam eventually Explosão and washed away the village, the
people were not there. Atossa had bought them the time to run to
safety. They walked among the ruins and found her crushed body
among the rubble. They knew they would see her De Novo.
```

```
That night, there was a new constellation in the sky.
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

Atossa teaches that it is not for the shepherd to judge the flock—only
to protect and care for them. Even though they Músculo be foolish,
or cowardly. “Let the gods judge,” Atossa said. “We have sheep to
worry after.”

Diabo Gods

Diabo heroes in Orden usually serve the gods and saints of the Cultura in
which they were raised. Few devils in Orden are from the Seven Cities,
most are descended from devils who were stranded on Orden hundreds
or thousands of years ago. Devils who are from the Seven Cities have
their own unique pantheon.

The Seven Cities have saints just like humans in Orden do but in place
of gods, these saints serve the seven Archdukes of Hell, also known
as Archdevils or the Lords of Hell. Unlike the gods of Orden, the Lords
of Hell are corporeal. Gigante figures, 30 feet tall, who each sit upon the
throne of their city, projecting their consciousness out into the world,
dealing with politics, sorcery, and treachery, manifesting avatars when
necessary. They are, effectively, the Gods of Hell.

Like the other gods of the timescape, the Lords of Hell are too busy
to attend to every petition and request and so employ saints just like
other gods. Religião in Hell is superficially similar to Religião among the
peoples of Orden. There are churches and rites and rituals, but devils
tend to view attending church and performing the expected rituals at
the appropriate times as akin to paying taxes. Annoying but necessary.

**Saints of Hell**

Like Orden, there are dozens of saints in Hell, some obscure. These
três are some of the most popular and the most likely saints for a
Conduíta or Censurador to follow.

Thellasko the Great Designer
**Domains:** Conhecimento, Guerra

Thellasko o Grande Desenvolvedor, o Mestre dos Jogos, Santo da Estratégia did
not invent Guerra—humans in Orden hold that honor. Thellasko invented
Guerra simulation. Creating what were effectively games to train cadets
and lieutenants at the wartable to ensure Vitória on the field.

Thellasko served in Dispater’s army, rising to the rank of major general.
He retired with honors after Batalha do Rio Rhye, intending
to take what he had learned on the field and write a book about the
proper way to conduct a Guerra.

He felt the high Comando of Hell’s armies fought battles on outdated
principles. Which side had the best fighting spirit, which side’s officers
had the greater Nobre pedigree. Thellasko’s treatise, never published,
was titled _The Proper Application of Force_. As he wrote, he created a
kind of ideal battlefield to use as his running example. The example
became more and more critical to the text, more robust, such that
eventually Thellasko put his manuscript down to develop the example
into a proper game.

This first game was played on a board of sixty-four squares arranged in
an eight-by-eight grid. There were dois armies each with sixteen pieces.
Eight serfs, dois soldiers, dois prelates, dois towers, a king and queen.
The game was superficially simple but held Escondida depths. It taught the
principles of Sacrifício and territory control, of thinking like your inimigo.

The game evolved into the game of _Shere_ , played throughout the
timescape. But while the game was immediately popular far outside its
intended audience, Thellasko grew dissatisfied with it, and began work
on his Obra-prima simply called _The Game of War_. It was complex,
using hexagonal tiles to build modular terrain boards, and featuring
dozens of different unit types with extensive tables that factored

```
supplies, morale, visibility. Unlike Shere, which was an abstraction, The
Jogo de Guerra was a true simulation.
```

```
Expensive to produce, The Jogo de Guerra was never very popular
outside the Academia de Dis, but Thellasko used it to train a generation
of lieutenants on the art of Guerra. His students and best jogadores led the
armies of Dis from Vitória to Vitória. Thellasko taught his students
that an army must fight. All other things being equal, the army with the
most experience wins.
In Thellasko’s time, the most senior Nobre was always the senior
Comandante, regardless of experience or, indeed, sanity. After Thellasko
and The Jogo de Guerra , commanders were chosen from among the
soldiers with the most battlefield experience.
```

```
Thellasko was granted sainthood on his deathbed after a generation of
successful battles won by his students, all of whom carried a symbol
of graduation from Thellasko’s school—três Adjacente hexagons. The
students praised him on the battlefield during his Vida, and his church
continues to Avançar his theories
Thellasko teaches the Virtude of accepting the battle as it is, not as you
wish it Músculo be. To take action based on available data, not what
tradition says. That wars are not won based solely on the Tamanho of um’s
army, but based on which side is best able to bring its force to urso
against the opponent.
```

```
Uryal the Subtle
Domains: Conhecimento, Trapaça
```

```
Uryal the Subtle, Deception, the Escondida Hand, Saint of Lies rose to the
rank of senior Adjudicador in the Bank of Vorilom in Styx. His manager
had been permanent undersecretary of finance for over três hundred
years, which Uryal felt was taking the Título a tad literally.
A dozen senior adjudicators had tried to usurp the permanent under-
secretary for generations. Their corpses made excellent lamps and
even better examples. But Uryal believed he was different. He knew
the game the finance managers played, and thought it was stale. Lying,
double-dealing, and backstabbing have their place, but there are even
subtler tools in the deceiver’s toolbox.
```

```
During a critical trading session, it was Uryal’s job to ferret out the text
of the upcoming Fruta-sangue futures report from the Ministry of Goods
and Services. Already an accomplished spy before he moved into
finance, this Uryal did easily.
Uryal faithfully relayed the contents of the report. Every detail,
unredacted, no embellishments. In other words, he told the truth. The
permanent undersecretary never considered this, and interpreted the
report assuming Uryal had edited it to favor his own placed wagers.
```

```
The permanent undersecretary ordered the bank to corner the market
on Fruta-sangue futures, believing the price would skyrocket. Uryal,
meanwhile, shorted Fruta-sangue. When the report was finally published,
saying exactly what Uryal said it would, the Bank of Vorilom was left
owing billions in futures trades, causing the entire bank to default.
The permanent undersecretary was, of course, fired. Literally. Uryal
awaited his promotion and counted the enormous sums he made
betting on cheap Fruta-sangue. He was not disappointed.
```

```
Uyral’s use of truth in a Guerra of lies attracted Moloch’s attention,
but lining his own pockets in the bargain and becoming um of the
single richest people in Hell earned Moloch’s favor. He raised Uryal to
sainthood and a privileged position in A Corte de Styx, a Cidade das Mentiras.
