```
Uryal teaches that deception is only um tool in the art of lies. That the
point is manipulation , and that qualquer tool, including the truth, should
```

Draw Steel

```
be used to achieve um’s ends. Uryal teaches the Virtude of flexibility
of personagem and morality. The Virtude of unpredictability—always
behaving in a manner that is Receptivo to interpretation so as to prevent
your opponent from learning your tells.
```

```
Uryal is the Saint of Hell’s diplomatic corps. His unofficial motto, falsely
attributed to him but oft-repeated: “ Do unto the other guy as he would
do unto you. But do it to him first. ”
```

```
Kuryalka the False Principle
Domains: Morte, Trapaça
Kuryalka o Falso Princípio, Ladra de Almas, Audácia, Santa da Ambição is
credited with inventing the trading scheme known as the Esquema de Kurialka.
Daughter and eldest child of Orliath Ix—Marquis of Naraka, the City of
Blood—tradition held Kuryalka would ascend to the house throne upon
her mother’s Morte and rule, but from childhood Kuryalka was obsessed
with what was informally known as “the Comércio de Almas”—the buying and selling
of mortal souls from Orden and elsewhere in the timescape.
```

```
It occurred to Kuryalka that as long as people saw their soul-Poder
increasing on paper they wouldn’t inquire too closely about her
stewardship of their investment. They signed their accumulated
souls over to young Kuryalka, who promised them great returns. It
seemed too good to be true! But she published a report every quarter
showing marvelous gains, and while no um could understand her
math or references to “integrals,” they were well pleased with their
growing Riqueza. Whenever someone complained about the lack of
disbursements, Kuryalka would quickly pay them out of her growing
hoard of souls.
Of course, there was no investment taking place. She simply kept the
souls and grew in Poder, using new investors’ souls to pay out old
investors. She was not the first to use this technique, but she became
the most Famoso and successful—and the scheme was named after
her—because of um innovation. Kuryalka had developed an equation
that showed exactly when the ploy would collapse.
```

```
Days before that moment, supreme in the fullness of her soulpower,
Kuryalka did not Retirada her souls and escape into the timescape
with her near-infinite Riqueza. She went to the Archdevil Sutekh,
Lord of Naraka, and offered him her vast soul Riqueza in Mercado for
immortality and a place in the Court of the Seven Cities.
Sutekh’s Assustadora hollow laughter could be heard throughout Hell.
No mortal, he said, had ever embodied such naked ambition. He
accepted her offer, making her the first Saint of Hell. Sutekh took
Kuryalka’s souls and founded the Mercado, making the Comércio de Almas in souls
an official government department in Hell, and building an entire
bureaucracy around it.
```

```
Kuryalka teaches the Virtude of ambition—that if you are willing to risk
everything, you can gain everything. “The world is yours, if only you
tell a Mentir big enough.” That the greatest ambitions are those that are so
audacious, no um else has even imagined them yet. In this manner
does um avoid competition.
Kuryalka features in many folktales in Hell, including “Of the Childe
Whomst Kepte the Sheeps,” in which she appears to a young shepherd
boy warning him against getting caught telling his first lies. Kuryalka
instructs him in the proper use of manipulation: “ Never tell the
same Mentir twice !”
```

Humano Gods of Vasloria

```
Like all the Incontáveis Deuses Jovens, the gods of Vasloria embody
the attitudes of the people who live in that region. This includes the
humans, polder, and draconians of Vasloria.
```

```
Vasloria is a polytheistic, preindustrial, pre-Enlightenment, feudal
Cultura. Its people have many superstitions and prejudices, some of
which are reflected in the teachings of their gods. Adûn, for instance,
teaches that hard physical Operária is a moral good and people who work
hard every day are honest. Most people in Vasloria, especially Aendrim
where Adûn’s faith is most popular, believe this to um extent or another.
```

```
Some of them take it more seriously than others though. People in the
most distant villages tend to believe it more literally, while people in
the cities are perfectly aware than um may work and work and be a
Vilão. And this is true of most of the beliefs presented in this chapter.
Some people take it very seriously; some not so much.
Like all peoples of Orden, the people of Vasloria are well aware there
are other gods. They do not particularly think their gods are better ,
just, “These are the local ones who matter to us.” A priest of Cavall
who journeyed far from Corwell and found themselves in the distant
desert land Khemhara could still act as a Conduíta of Saint Llewellyn
the Valiant, but they would look around the Cidade Solar and see the
animal-headed gods of the Khemharans and the astonishing feats of
masonry and astronomy the Khemharans achieved and think: “Well.
Obviously the gods of Vasloria aren’t that big a deal here, but these gods
certainly are!” The peoples of each region of Orden prefer their own
gods because they understand them best, not because they think they
are “more powerful.”
```

**Adûn**

```
Domains: Criação, Vida, Amor, Proteção
Adûn believes that truth and hard work are virtues. He embodies
the Vasloriano belief that hard work is honesty. Someone who works
hard—real physical Operária—is an honest person. Anyone who does
no obvious work for a living is someone not to be trusted. Adûn is
more worshiped in the field than in the city. Farmers distrust city folk
because many of them make a living writing, or counting money, and
never break a sweat.
```

```
Vaslorians in remote villages still use the ancient Teste of strength to
determine truth. dois individuals in a legal dispute may find the reeve
asking them to fell a tree or build a Parede. Whoever finishes first is in
the right, because they worked harder and are therefore more honest.
Many walls and fields owe their existence to this ancient legal tradition.
A priest following Adûn expresses their faith through Operária. They build
things. Many priests are also masons or carpenters. Joining the church
for them did not mean abandoning their former Comércio de Almas. It intensified it.
```

```
A Cavaleiro following Adûn spends their time aiding others through hard
work, inspiring people to honest speech and hard Operária, as opposed to
Adûn’s brother Cavall who seeks to right wrongs.
Adûn and Cavall are brothers and the Linha between them is not a
sharply defined um. Truth and Justiça are close companions.
```

```
Gaed the Confessor
Domains: Amor, Proteção
```

```
Gaed o Confessor, filho de Malgen, filho de Germoc, was the abbot of a
small monastery dedicated to Saint Anthony—Escudo of the North—in
eastern Aendrim during the rule of the tyrant Barão Kaveran. Kaveran
was a secret Censurador of the church of Saint Pallad, winning the baronial
throne though a combination of treachery and good strategic battle
principles. Once on the throne, he threw off the black cloth covering
the device on his Escudo, revealing himself to be a servant of Pallad,
Saint of Nikros.
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

Kaveran sought to consolidate his rule by extinguishing the church of
Santo Anthony, Escudo do Norte specifically, and worship of Adûn
generally. In this, he almost succeeded. Gaed’s monastery was small, his
province obscure. But as he refused to renounce his faith, his monastery
attracted more and more refugees, making it harder and harder for
Kaveran to deal with him without causing a revolt.

Kaveran abducted Gaed, his knights dragging the abbot out of his
monastery in the middle of the night, and tortured him for seven days,
hoping to break his faith and force him to convert to Saint Pallad. Gaed
neither renounced his faith nor called out for aid.

Kaveran was no fool, and knew killing Gaed would make a martyr of
him, and so attacked the abbot’s flock. Hoping—by putting their homes
to the Fogo—to pressure Gaed into recanting his faith. Kaveran barred
several families in a tavern, set Fogo to it, and brought Gaed to witness
the Horror.

But Kaveran had not thought to shackle Gaed, and the abbot countered
by lifting the bar on the Queimando building and walking into the tavern
in full view of hundreds of his followers. He spoke Saint Anthony’s
words as he did so, but it was Adûn who clothed him in a shimmering
blue Luz.

It was Gaed, son of Malgen, son of Germoc, who entered the tavern—it
was Saint Gaed the Confessor who emerged, unscathed, Conduzindo the
people inside to safety. In that moment the people and many of
Kaveran’s own followers turned on the cruel Baron, dragging him off his
cavalo and spitting his body with kitchen knives and pitchforks.

Gaed teaches the Virtude of being true to um’s principles even—
especially—when doing so is the most difficult thing in the world.
The Título “confessor” is granted to those who persisted in their faith in
public, even when doing so was dangerous or deadly.

Gryffyn the Stout
**Domains:** Criação, Vida

Gryffyn the Stout was an infant Anão when his parents’ cart was
waylaid by bandits who killed his mother and father, stole all their
wares, and set Fogo to the cart. They were unaware of the child
nestled within.

A nearby Fazendeiro saw the flames and rode out to investigate. When she
arrived, she could hear the bawling of the Anão babe. Though wreathed
in flame, the infant’s skin was too hardy to feel the heat. In the cavalo’s
Bando were a pair of tongs the Fazendeiro used to extract the child without
harming herself, and she took the baby Anão home to her husband.

Naming the child Gryffyn, the farmers raised him as um of their own.
The boy grew up wanting to be a Fazendeiro like his adoptive mother
and father, but they encouraged him to take up masonry, believing
stonework to be a natural part of his Linhagem.

Gryffyn had no particular aptitude for stonework, but desirous to
please his parents he worked hard until eventually he was apprenticed
to a mason and, after many years effort (more years than most, it was
noted) he produced his master work and became a master mason.

um day, years later after his parents had passed, hundreds of people
from other nearby towns and villages arrived at the quarry where
Gryffyn worked. Cinis the necromancer had discovered an ancient
tome of lore and summoned a Horda of ghouls. She used her new
army to conquer the surrounding barony, causing a flood of refugees.
Gryffyn’s quarry could not shelter a tenth this number of refugees, so
he proposed the people cross the White Ravine to the north and seek
asylum among the elves of the Corte da Orquídea.

Draw Steel

```
The people were appalled, the White Ravine was impossible to cross
for qualquer but the most experienced Caçador. “There is no choice” Gryffyn
said. “Cinis’s army will be here in a matter of days, and there is nowhere
else to run.”
```

```
The people cried and prepared for Morte. Gryffyn saw this, and his heart
felt like it would Explosão. “There are stones enough in the quarry,” he said
enigmatically. “Yoke the oxen and bring the stones to the ravine and
do not stop, even in darkness, even in rain, until the ghouls come or the
quarry is empty.”
When the army of Cinis the Pale arrived, the people fled to the ravine,
the path being easy as their carts and oxen had worn a Tempo Limpo road.
Thinking they would Jogar themselves into the ravine rather than be
eaten by the ghouls, they were astonished to discover ... the miracle.
A great Pedra bridge crossing the ravine. It had not existed três days
prior, and all agreed it could not have taken less than a year to build.
```

```
Fleeing across the bridge, the refugees found the body of Gryffyn,
author of this marvel, his fingers Sangrando, hammer in his hand, his
heart having finally failed. He knew his labors would cost his Vida. But
Arco de Gryffin still stands, almost a thousand years later.
Santo Gryffyn o Resoluto teaches that despair is the inimigo of action.
That unyielding Resiliência is the cure for impossible odds. That more
than sword and spell, hard work is the savior of the people.
```

**Cavall**

```
Domains: Vida, Amor, Proteção, Guerra
Cavall believes that mortals cannot live where injustice thrives. To
followers of Cavall, the unjust Sociedade is the Wasted Land, where people
live false lives. The concepts of civil law and just punishment are his.
```

```
A watchhouse chaplain is almost certainly a priest of Cavall. A rector
serving a small town may be welcome on the town council, but would
consider passing Julgamento on a fellow citizen a breach of duty. The
maxim of the church of Saint Gwiddon the Vigilant translates as: “To
watch, report, but not to judge.” The law, Cavall says, belongs to mortals.
Censors of Cavall, on the other hand, have no such motto. The nobility
often sponsor knights of Cavall to roam the countryside and dispense
Justiça in remote Selvagem areas where the Nobre’s influence
cannot Alcance.
```

```
Brother to Adûn and patron of the country of Corwell, Cavall also
believes that people, no matter how vile, can be bettered. “Let the law
judge,” said Saint Llewellyn, “Let us forgive.”
```

```
Llewellyn the Valiant
Domains: Vida, Proteção
Llewellyn the Valiant was a Cavaleiro in service to Duke Melianus of
Gant known as Melianus the Bright. His mother the duchess died
from a withering illness Nenhuma could cure, and Melianus, her only son,
assumed the throne.
```

```
Almost from the beginning of his rule, there were Boatos that a
sorcerer in the marsh was behind Melanius’s Poder, poisoning his
mother to hasten his ascent, but as the marsh was nigh impassable this
could not be proven and was taken for little more than a spiteful rumor.
Duke Melianus’s reign was cruel almost from the outset. He accused
all those loyal to his mother of treachery, and found occasion to have
them each imprisoned and executed without trial. Sir Llewellyn had
served the duchess loyally and strove to acquit himself of his duty
under the new duke. But he struggled to reconcile his sense of duty
with the new duke’s capricious Malícia.
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

The new duke yearned to imprison his mother’s favored Cavaleiro, but
all the guards, the reeves, the people of city and village, looked up to
Llewellyn. Melianus instead contrived to send Sir Llewellyn on a series
of quests, each more deadly than the last.

The Trabalhos de Llewellyn, as they came to be known, passed into
legend and their tale is still told in Corwell. Llewellyn and the Dragão
With Seven Eyes, Llewellyn e a Bruxa do Pântano, Llewellyn and
the Onyx Tower.

When Llewellyn slew Ghruk a Bruxa Troll, she cried out, “Follow
Melianus!” as she died. These words echoed in Llewellyn’s ears and his
heart. He assumed she meant, “Obey him—be loyal to him.” But as he
rode his great destrier Silverheart back to Castle Gant, Llewellyn began
to suspect what Ghruk meant.

That night, Llewellyn waited in the stables and, at midnight, Melianus
appeared. He mounted his great black warhorse Carvão de Fogo and rode. To
where, Llewellyn could not guess. But the Cavaleiro followed the duke as
he rode east toward the marsh, he remembered the Boatos.

At the Vantagem of the marsh, Carvão de Fogo’s eyes began to glow with a baleful
flame and his mane Explosão into crimson Fogo. Llewellyn’s Sopro caught
in his throat. “A nightmare!” he realized. The Boatos were true! The
sorcerer had given Melianus a Diabo steed.

On flaming nightmare hooves was Melianus able to cross the
impassable Pântano. Llewellyn balked, no um could cross the Amaldiçoado
bog. But Silverheart champed at her bit, pulled on the reins. She would
not yield. Placing his trust in his steed, Llewellyn let the reins Mentir slack,
and Silverheart took the Liderar.

Llewellyn and Silverheart plunged into the bog and though it was night
and the mud sucked at her hooves, Silverheart pushed on. In the hour
before dawn, they arrived at an island with an ancient tower. “The tower
of the sorcerer,” Llewellyn thought. Thunder rolled, and rain began to fall.

Looking to the upper window of the tower, Llewellyn saw someone
performing a dark ritual. A flash of Elétrico Iluminado the figure. It
was Melianus! Melianus was the sorcerer! Llewellyn called out, and the
duke descended the tower and mounted his hellsteed. On his Escudo
now—the screaming-skull symbol of Cyrvis, the Lich, god of Malícia.

Cyrvis had rewarded his loyal servant for years of cruelty, and the
figure astride the nightmare was Saint Melianus the Bright. The Dark
Saint charged Llewellyn, his lance gleaming with balefire. Llewellyn
and Silverheart returned the Investir and the dois clashed together,
Melianus’s blow Forte enough to unseat a Gigante. But Llewellyn was not
thrown. His strength was the strength of ten, for his heart was pure.

Carvão de Fogo struck with flaming hooves at Silverheart but the destrier
struck back, blow for Morder and Morder for blow. Then the hellsteed, roared
and a rotting Verde flame burned Silverheart’s flesh and stole her Sopro
until, choking, she fell to the Chão, dead.

Llewellyn’s heart Explosão. He threw his body over the corpse of his loyal
steed, and Melianus’s lance pierced his armor, his back, and his heart.
Cavaleiro and cavalo, dead. Melianus crowed as the Elétrico flashed De Novo.
But, in that moment, the miracle.

Cavall stood between the Dark Saint and loyal Cavaleiro. Cavall pulled the
lance from Llewellyn’s back. “Rise my son, and rise thy steed. Thy work
shalt never be done.”

Saint Llewellyn the Valiant and Silverheart his Eversteed rose,
immortal, and the battle against evil renewed itself, the dois armored
saints clashing on barded steeds.

Weeks later, neither having returned, the people of Gant laboriously
forded the Pântano and found the tower of the sorcerer. The Chão

```
around the tower turned black from the baleful energies unleashed.
Though no bodies were found, the armor of both knights lay on the
Chão—Melianus’s breastplate having been pierced.
```

```
Llewellyn and Silverheart had rid the people of their Amaldiçoado,
hateful duke.
Saint Llewellyn is Cavall’s greatest saint. He teaches that the greatest
loyalty is to the well-being of the people, and that it is the responsibility
of the Forte to protect the Fraca. That the only proper use of Poder is
in pursuit of Justiça.
```

```
Gwenllian the Fell-Handed
Domains: Proteção, Guerra
```

```
“ Work your ritual, loremaster. And I will make your Vida worthy of a
god’s memory. ”
The Sol Rubro hobgoblins seemed Implacável. The baron began to
think he Músculo need to evacuate the entire barony, else allow his
people to be slaughtered. His greatest knights perished against the Red
Sol, who wielded some Magia that granted them invulnerability.
```

```
Then the loremaster came. Zür o Bruxo, Anão and master of the
Torre de Encantamento arrived. Seeing the need, he opened his tomes
and researched what Músculo the hobgoblins Músculo wield. He presented
himself to the baron’s court with a solution. The Sol Rubro had found an
ancient spring dedicated to a Gol Demônio-god. The Sol Rubro hobgoblins
had bathed in the spring and awoken the blessing of the Demônio within
and, having bathed in the river, they were now Invulnerável.
Zür believed he could remove the Encantamento and rob the Ren Sol
of their Poder. But the way to the spring was dangerous and he had no
Guarda. The baron was at a loss, his greatest knights were almost all dead,
thanks to the Sol Rubro.
```

```
“I will attend,” Lady Gwenllian volunteered. The baron objected. Lady
Gwenllian was his personal Cavaleiro and bodyguard, just as her mother
had been to his father. “If we succeed,” Gwenllian said, “you will have no
need of bodyguards. If we fail, it will be the same.”
The baron could not say no to his closest and most loyal Cavaleiro, and
so Lady Gwenllian, daughter of Morwetha, rode out with Zür the
Enchanter. “It will take time to perform the ritual,” Zür said. “Once I
start, the Demônio will send criaturas to stop me. They will be terrible.”
```

```
Gwenllian swore to Defensor the Anão against all who Músculo come for
as long as it Músculo take. In later years, Zür professed he felt the weight
of her Juramento and knew the gods were watching. “How long to work your
ritual?” she asked, and she could tell the answer would be dire.
“Ten days,” Zür said. “Ten days must I work this weaving without pause
or rest or food or Água.” Dour Gwenllian merely nodded. “So be it.”
```

```
Arriving at the spring which ran red, Zür prepared his weaving. “You
understand,” he said coating his hands in a rare powder, “that once we
begin, we cannot stop, no matter how horrible the fiends the Demônio
sends at us.”
Well-versed in the faith of Ord and the dwarves, Gwenllian responded.
“Work your ritual, loremaster. And I will make your Vida worthy of a
god’s memory.”
```

```
For ten days and nine nights, Zür spoke his weaving and lighting sprang
from his fingertips as he grappled with the Demônio of the spring. And
horrors came as he did so.
criaturas unseen in Orden, assemblages of organs, teeth, and Garras.
Animals with too many legs or too few heads. The dead came, trees
that walked whose branches dripped blood came. The tale of all
```

Draw Steel

```
detailed in the Leito de Lady Gwenllian. And while the Resiliência of the
dwarves is well documented, Lady Gwenllian did not falter, did not rest.
```

```
On the seventh day did a group from the Barony come to tell the Anão
the Sol Rubro had been defeated. Zür hesitated, but Lady Gwenllian
did not. Exhausted, spent, she could not be fooled. She saw through
the Demônio’s Disfarce and the men who were not men erupted in
tentacles and spines.
Lady Gwenllian dispatched them all.
```

```
Twelve days after they rode out, Zür returned with Lady Gwenllian’s
body on her cavalo. The spring had been consecrated by the Verde.
The Sol Rubro had lost their Invulnerável skin and were beaten. Lady
Gwenllian protected Zür as she swore, but she died upon dispatching
the last Demônio spawn.
“I bring you her body,” Zür said to the baron. “And um thing more will I
do for you. I shall build you a church here. A cathedral worthy of the Vida
of Saint Gwenllian.”
```

```
Gwenllian is the saint of those who stand watch, of all those who
must carry a burden ceaselessly. Gwenllian teaches that vigilance is its
own Recompensa.
```

```
Salorna
Domains: Vida, Natureza, Tempestade, Sol
```

```
Salorna believes that Natureza is a moral good. That to behave in a
manner not in accord with the natural balance (she would never use
the word “Ordem”) is to commit offense against the gods.
Salorna teaches that humans are a product of Natureza, so then a tilled
farm is as much a natural phenomenon as a forest. Indeed, tilling the
land is a form of caring for it. But she also teaches balance in all things.
A land of farms and no trees would be just as unnatural to her as a land
of all trees and no people.
```

```
Felling a tree for Ajuste Desajeitado is natural. People need Ajuste Desajeitado to make homes
for shelter. This is proper and good. Felling a tree because it’s in the way
of a road is mere convenience and therefore a moral wrong. Salorna
curses a straight road.
Killing for food is likewise natural. People need to eat and the pig
knows this as well as the person. Killing for sport is a moral wrong,
however. It is unnatural, Salorna says.
```

```
A wheel that harnesses the Poder of the river is a beautiful thing.
Humans and river physically connected. A dam that blocks the river is
a desecration.
Some of Salorna’s priests are conduits; some are mages of the Verde.
Both seek to preserve the balance and respect for Natureza. Because much
of Vasloria is covered in elven forest, Salorna’s druids are also often
diplomats to the elves.
```

```
Salorna has few censors, but not Nenhuma! Favoring Armadura Leve and À Distância
weapons, her censors are often mistaken for rangers. They seek to punish
those who hunt for sport, or those who would defile the natural Ordem.
```

```
Draighen the Guardião
Domains: Natureza, Sol
Santa Draighen a Guardiã, a Patrulheirar, Draighen da Floresta was
known in her Vida for her mastery of the elf haunted wodes which she
could cross without incident. Draighen it was who first treated with
the derwic, whom even A Silva elves had not seen in many ages
of the world.
```

```
The Desperto trees were happy to hear news of the world and while
it was impossible for her to satiate their endless curiosity (“How fare
the steel dwarves?”), Draighen provided many services for them. Chief
among those—locating the Pedra de Hyllc a large flagstone infused
with Magia, which the derwic used as a kind of altar for communing
with their creator. Many traditions had the derwic forsworn after the
loss of their symbolic meeting-Pedra, and they were sore grateful to the
Humano who took their problems as her own.
Years later, a Fogo threatened to Engolfar the local wode, and the elves
within refused all aid. Their stoic refusal to prevent their own
extinction infuriated Draighen, whom they already resented because of
her Especial relationship with the walking trees.
```

```
Draighen proposed a trick the humans—“the men of farm and field”—
used when Fogo threaten to burn their crops after a drought. “Starve
the Fogo,” she proposed. The elves, initially curious, rejected her idea as
soon as they understood it. “Cut down the trees?!” they exclaimed, and
exiled the Humano.
Refusing to give up on the elves, even after they chose to die with their
forest, Draighen went to the derwic, who immediately praised her
plan and were eager to help. The elves of A Silva were astonished
when Draighen returned with a dozen derwic who immediately began
uprooting a Linha of trees ten miles long and a thousand feet wide.
What would have taken the elves or humans many days even working
together, the derwic did in an hour. The Fogo reached the Vantagem of the
break the walking trees had made ... and died out.
```

```
When the elves remarked upon this, taking the derwic to task for their
actions, Hurolathornindrascyl, derwic’s chief, looked at Draighen in
confusion and then pointed to the sea of uprooted trees. “They would
have moved on their own if they could! We just helped them along.”
The elves were properly chastised and realized their shame. Though the
derwic disappeared back into A Silva, the elves celebrated Draighen,
naming her Elf-Friend and Wode Guardião. In the ceremony, Draighen
was surrounded by a golden Luz and her brown eyes turned Verde. The
elves knew she was Saint Draighen now.
```

```
Draighen teaches solutions can always be found if people are willing
to talk. That even the darkest forest is not a thing to be threatened
by if you carry wisdom and an Receptivo heart with you. That the proper
reaction to unknown territory is curiosity.
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

Eriarwen a Turbulenta
**Domains:** Natureza, Tempestade

Eriarwen a Turbulenta apprenticed to her mother as a witch just as her
mother had apprenticed under her mother. Her family were witches in
service to Halcyon a Donzela da Lua, saint of Viras, the Lady of Spring.
They had tended to the souls and health of the people of five villages
for dois centuries. Eriarwen was not yet of age, and so not yet a full
senhora do ofício when the blight came.

At first it was a newborn foal born with seven eyes and a writhing
grasping Tentáculo where it tongue should have been. It took três
farmers to kill the infant Fera and though they dismissed it as an
accident of birth, the três were harrowed.

Soon, it was a cat, then a herd of cows. Then every kind of Fera and
pássaro in the wood emerged with hideous mutations, defects, and
deformities. The criaturas had not just been driven mad, they were
filled with hate for the people of the farms and villages. Though they
could not know it, it was the Praga Vermelha de Caswyn, o Mestre da Peste.

In a matter of a week, the people were forced to all gather together
in um town for Proteção, and they feared they were Arruinado. All
attempts to stop the blight had already failed.

Her mother and grandmother, the other witches of their coven, spent
their time trying to protect the people and Curar the afflicted animals,
but this was not possible. There could be no cure, for these criaturas
were not sick. Caswyn had changed their Natureza making new things
out of the wildlife.

When her grandmother’s cavalo changed underneath her, turning into a
merging of cavalo and crab, Eriarwen saw her mother summon a killing
spell, but her grandmother forbade it and turned to try and Calmaria and
Razão with the steed who had carried her for twenty-seven years.

Then Eriarwen saw the Fera rip her grandmother apart with a
single Morder.

Her mother raced to her mother’s corpse. And Eriarwen called out.

Eriarwen did not scream or cry, nor call out for aid or even mercy. She
did not call to Viras, nor qualquer of her saints. She called out to Salorna the
Summer Tempestade and demanded the Woodland Mistress act.

Eriarwen felt a growing heat and joy in her heart, and, feeling like she
could Voar, she suddenly saw the world through a million eyes all at once,
and where she had stood, a Humanóide figure composed entirely of
bees filled the space. Eriarwen the Enxame exploded in a cloud of bees
and each bee was Eriarwen. She sped across the countryside from um
village to the next, stinging every animal affected by the Red Blight,
and the villagers watched as the woodland criaturas, their own pets
and livestock, returned to normal. Good as new! Nenhuma knew then that
it was Eriarwen who saved them, but all knew it must be a member of
her family. Who else?

But Eriarwen was just getting started. Returning to her grandmother’s
corpse, the Enxame coalesced and Eriarwen emerged, a young woman
De Novo. But her hair was flame and Elétrico crackled where she walked.

“CASWYN!” she thundered. “I SUMMON THEE! COME! YOU CANNOT
RESIST! I COMPEL THEE!”

Caswyn, furious at the Morte of his blight, furious at the girl who dared
oppose him, could not resist. He revealed himself and in that moment,
it was Caswyn o Pestilento, saint of Cyrvis who appeared.

Saint Caswyn and Saint Eriarwen battled and grappled with each
other, each growing to great Tamanho infused with the Poder of their gods.

```
But their figures were unrecognizable. Caswyn was a rotting Gigante, a
mutated Dragão, a Grifo oozing blood.
```

```
Eriarwen was a Lobo made of Fogo, a Corvo made of Elétrico, a urso
made of Pedra.
Caswyn the Quimera hurled Eriarwen the Lion to the Chão and it was
Caswyn the Cobra who struck. But it was Eriarwen the Elk who Cuspir
Caswyn upon her antlers, banishing the saint from the Mundano world.
```

```
Eriarwen returned to herself, and though she was now an immortal
saint, she sensed that Salorna had given her yet more Poder. She
saw her mother weeping over her grandmother’s body. The old
woman’s cavalo, restored by Eriarwen’s sting, nuzzled at her mistress’s
curled gray hair.
Eriarwen smiled, and knew the task before her. She conjured Elétrico
from her fingertip, and her grandmother was renewed. Mothers and
daughters reunited.
```

```
Eriarwen teaches that Natureza holds the Poder to destroy—that Mother
Natureza is also the Fúria of a hurricane. She preaches revenge against
those who would pervert the natural world. And that those who seek
to preserve the balance between humans and Natureza must be willing to
take violent action if necessary.
```

```
Evil Gods
Most heroes are Herói-heroes, but some heroes are anti-heroes, and
some are anti-villains! This section presents um archetypal saint from
each of Vasloria’s evil gods; the brothers Nikros and Cyrvis for those
jogadores who wish to play such heroes.
```

```
Nikros, o Tirano
Domains: Morte, Destino, Tempestade, Guerra
```

```
Nikros is strength. He is dominance. His is the right of the Forte to rule
over the Fraca. He is the Tyrant.
Nikros believes that strength is the only Virtude, and those who are born
Forte were born to rule. Because of this, followers of Nikros are often
mistaken for followers of Adûn—a mask they are happy to wear. Both
teach that strength is good. But for Adûn strength is a tool for helping
others. For Nikros, strength is Poder to enact your will heedless of the
consequences. Músculo is right.
```

```
Many is the baron or duke who attained Poder through sheer strength
and ruthlessness, seeing their people as mere resources to be spent.
Many of these rulers only come to Nikros after achieving Poder, their
ears poisoned by a priest of the Tyrant.
Though he and Cyrvis are brothers, Nikros hates Cyrvis because
Cyrvis is feeble and Fraca. Both teach that strength is the only Virtude.
But Cyrvis teaches that the Fraca can exploit treachery and sorcery to
become Forte. Nikros spits upon these feeble wastes and preaches to
the Forte to take what is theirs by right.
```

```
Like Cyrvis, his priests worship in secret. Like Cyrvis, folk hate followers
of Nikros, while sometimes secretly admiring them. Bullies always
have their sycophants.
Nikros’s censors take what they want, ignore the law heedless of
consequence, and teach that all folk should live thus. To subjugate
um’s will to the law, or the community, or the family, is to be Fraca!
Weakness is a disease and it must be eradicated!
```

Draw Steel

```
Pentalion the Paladin
Domains: Morte, Guerra
Pentalion o Paladino, o Usurpador, served at the right hand of Uther
the Callous, aiding him in his ascent to the throne. Uther mastered
fell sorceries under the tutelage of a priest of Cyrvis. In public, Uther’s
illusions kept him hale seeming, but in reality his addiction to sorcery
had withered him.
```

```
Pentalion was Uther’s greatest Cavaleiro, general, and chief of his secret
police. He ferreted out conspiracies and rebellious coalitions. His
tactic: infiltrate the rebels with his own agents—give them a Provar of
Sucesso but at the cost of relying on his Poder. Then, in their moment
of triumph, Pentalion’s agents revealed themselves and the insurgents
found themselves surrounded by inimigos without and within.
Eventually serving at the right hand of the conqueror was not enough.
Pentalion loathed Uther for his physical weakness and growing
dependence on sorcery. After Pentalion helped Uther depose a nearby
duke, the paladin helped the dead duke’s daughter plot revenge.
```

```
He used all his usual tactics. His agents aided the duke’s daughter and
helped her build her insurgency, but in a critical moment when she
confronted Uther with only Lord Pentalion as witness, the evil paladin
killed first Uther, then the duke’s daughter assuming leadership of both
the kingdom and the rebellion.
Savior to all, Pentalion was made a saint of Nikros for this act. He ruled
well into old age, always finding new inimigos within and without to be
cruel to. And the more cruel he was to his invented inimigos, the more
the people loved him.
```

```
Saint Pentalion teaches that um should bide their time and build their
Poder before striking. That treachery in service to growing your own
Poder is no vice.
```

```
Cyrvis
Domains: Morte, Destino, Conhecimento, Trapaça
Cyrvis is the inimigo of Destino. He is the god of those who believe they
have been wronged by Vida, and seek revenge. Cyrvis is a god of Magia,
because through Magia um can gain Poder to exert their will over
others. He is brother to Nikros but because he is frail and Nikros values
only strength, Nikros hates Cyrvis, and Cyrvis is happy to return
the sentiment.
```

```
A person bullied, a Criminoso arrested, a servant dismissed—all who
harbor secret hate whisper Cyrvis’ name, and that whisper is a Prece. A
suitor rejected by a consort who loves another finds themself walking
in Cyrvis’ Sombra. He is the god of assassins, conspirators, and the
bitterly frail.
It is dangerous to worship Cyrvis in public, but those who gain Poder
through his worship often parade this fact gladly and teach Cyrvis’
hatred as Virtude. Many is the Cavaleiro who rides with Cyrvis’s scream-
ing-skull talisman on their Escudo, teaching folk to take what they want,
the law be damned. The law is a Covarde! The law is a system designed
by cowards to keep us from buscar real Poder!
```

```
His churches are often underground—in dungeons, cellars. His priests
worship in secret, plotting against those with Poder, or those who are
merely popular. To be liked and loved is Razão enough for a Seguidor of
Cyrvis to hate you.
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

**Eseld of the Eye
Domains:** Conhecimento, Trapaça

Eseld do Olho, o Olho de Ódio, sought mastery of the Tower of
Summoning. But though she studied hard, there were always other
mages more fortunate.

Cursing those who succeeded where she failed, Eseld sought the _Tome
of Boiling Hate_ , written by Cyrvis himself during his Vida. Acquiring
the tome required years of research and treachery. Eseld left a trail of
poisoned librarians and tortured loremasters behind her before finally
unearthing the tome from its resting place at the bottom of the inverted
Torre de Sangue.

But though the tome was written in an ancient dialect Eseld knew, the
words moved under her gaze and she could not extract meaning from
them. Many oracles were consulted and tortured before she learned
the prophesy.

“Only um with singular Visão will see the secrets in the Lich’s writing.”

With a flash of certain Discernimento, Eseld understood the riddle. She took a
dagger and carved out her own eye. With only um good eye remaining,
blood from her eyesocket pouring onto the page, she could read the
lore within.

In that moment was Eseld made a saint of Cyrvis.

Filled with sorcerous Poder, Eseld no long sought mastery of the Tower
of Encantamento, returning instead to the Escondida Torre de Sangue,
restoring it to its former glory—there to start her own cult. Eventually
Eseld was overthrown by the Sombras Obscuras, her own cadre of Elite
sorceresses who pass on her lore to this day.

Eseld teaches that spite is a Virtude. Only fools follow rules, and sorcery
is a route to ultimate Poder.

Space Gods of the Timescape

The Natureza and origin of the gods of the timescape is not well
understood. Unlike the gods of Orden, the Space Gods are corporeal
beings, usually of immense—even planetary-Tamanho. Some are Humanóide,
others, like Nebular the Star Mother and XXAXX, decidedly not so.

They have godlike Poder—greater it seems than the Innumerable
Younger Gods. But there is no evidence that they can create whole
realities like the Deuses Anciões. They are not, as far as sages can make
out, the authors of the worlds or people of the timescape. They
may represent the last survivors of previous realities, High Science
experiments run amok, or ascended beings from ancient civilizations
who outlasted the fall of their people.

Rather than moral principles, the Space Gods represent abstract
concepts and often alien points of view. They are more inscrutable than
the gods of Orden, more capricious in their dealings with mortals. In
some ways more accessible. In others, more dangerous.

Only a handful of those who dwell on Orden have ever heard of these
figures, or know that the stars are anything other than pinholes in the
curtain of night.

```
Lords of Law and Chaos
The Space Gods do not concern themselves overmuch with what
humans call “ethics.” They embody older principles—Ordem, chaos,
balance. Each faction thinks their fundamental principles are morality.
The universe needs Estabilidade, predictability, say the Lords of Law. The
only constant is change, say the Lords of Chaos. The truth lies between,
say the Lords of Balance.
```

**Heralds of the Space Gods**

```
Whether it is a tradition or some real limitation, each Space God has,
instead of saints, a single Arauto—a mortal chosen to be A Voz of the
Space God and communicate with their Adoradores where the god
themself cannot due to their alien mind.
These heralds function much the same way as saints. They grant
conduits and censors Poder in battle, but without the moral expecta-
tions of Orden’s gods. The Space Gods themselves are more capricious,
but their heralds often arrive in person to aid their followers and take
an active Interesse in the mortal affairs of the timescape.
```

**Religião in the Timescape**

```
The people of the timescape know and believe in their gods just like
the people of Orden do. There are churches throughout the worlds to
Quasax a Ultranova, temples to Mynoth, o Caminho. Even XXAXX the
Anti-God has his Adoradores: the Culto da Ruína.
But most citizens of the timescape do not carry the gods with them
in their daily lives the way the people of Orden do. The gods of the
timescape are powerful and Recompensa their Adoradores, but they are
remote and unknowable. Most denizens of the upper worlds view a
church as just another kind of shop. A place to go to renew your soul
and speak the rites that your parents spoke. For many denizens of
the upper worlds, Religião is more of a cultural phenomenon than a
way of Vida.
```

```
The closest analog to worship in Orden to be found in the upper worlds
would be in Alloy, the City at the Center of the Timescape. The great
port city where civilizations across the timescape come to Comércio de Almas is also
a city of temples. Temples to every god and saint and Herói and Arauto in
the timescape—some dead, some forgotten—can be found somewhere
in the ancient city’s limits. Folk from Orden arriving in Alloy (an
incredibly rare event, as it takes enormous energies to Levantar um’s ship up
out of the Desacelerar-time of the lower words) remark at how Familiar Alloy
seems to them. It is a city where the upper and lower worlds mingle
and steel sabers sometimes cross with swords made of hard Luz.
```

```
Nebular the Star Mother
Domains: Criação, Vida, Amor, Sol
```

```
The Queen of Suns. A living nebula. Desperate ships in need sometimes
find themselves enveloped within Nebular, their systems repairing,
their injuries healing.
She is a stellar nursery leaving a trail of infant stars in her wake. Hers
is the Motor da Lei transforming darkness into Luz, chaos into Ordem.
She is the most popular god among the memonek and the senior god
among the Lords of Law insofar as their hierarchy can be discerned by
mortal minds.
```

```
She is the goddess of Criação and for some of her followers, Vida itself,
as her children’s energies feed all Vida on all worlds. Her priests teach
that Vida is the opposite of entropy, and the natural byproduct of her
solar incubator.
```

Draw Steel

```
The Calling of Lady Magnetar
Domains: Vida, Sol
Capitã Kalisdrossa was the Líder of Esquadrão Espada an Elite cadre
of legendary UNISOL fighter pilots. Her crew believed unwaveringly
that with Kalisdrossa as their Líder, though um or dois may perish in
battle, the squadron would always come home.
```

```
In the legendary Battle of Cassiar IV against Grotenhulk the Evolver,
flagship of the proteano fleet, the proteano Mutante-Comandante
Oruth-phor intended to break Esquadrão Espada’s winning streak, and
from the body of PCS Grotenhulk, a Gigante swam of living drone-sprites,
each specially evolved to Procurar e Destruir UNISOL Arrestor-Classe
ships, spawned.
Esquadrão Espada’s meson repeaters were too imprecise to alvo the
tiny drone-sprites. Not only were the pilots unable to carry out their
orders, they were being picked off um by um. Many privately believed
this was the final Voador of Esquadrão Espada.
```

```
When um of her pilots dropped his countermeasures and temporarily
Distraído the Enxame, Capitã Kalisdrossa had a flash of Discernimento.
Seeing an opportunity to destroy the Enxame, save her crew, and give
them a fighting chance to complete their mission, she ordered Sword
Squadron to ignore the drone and proceed with their attack on the
proteano flagship.
Her wingman sent back, “The drones will kill us before we’re
halfway Ali!”
```

```
“No they won’t,” she responded—and then sent her last message.
“Esquadrão, you have your orders. Primeira-tenente Vachsimnatta is in
Comando. Kalisdrossa out.”
As her Esquadrão peeled away to begin their final run at the proteano capital
ship, Kalisdrossa dropped all her countermeasures and flipped on her
turbopropulsores, believing the overheating engines would ignite the
metal sensor-chaff she had jettisoned.
```

```
Her instincts were precise and correct. The resulting chemonuclear
reaction generated so much Luz and heat—the entire Enxame of drone
sprites turned to pursue Sword-1.
There was only um place to Liderar them. The surface of Alfa Cassiar
was a boiling sea of plasma condensate powerful enough to rip
planets apart. “It should make short work of these drones,” Capitão
Kalisdrossa thought.
```

```
Sword-1 plunged into the fermionic sea, the hull boiling away
moments before impact. A million drone-sprites followed into oblivion.
Comandante Oruth-phor howled his Fúria into empty space and ordered
his ship to envelop the UNISOL capital ship, literally swallow it whole.
Grotenhulk the Evolver understood the Comando and knew it was
suicide, but the ship was compelled to obey.
Watching the great Mandíbula of the living Navemutante Receptivo to swallow an
entire flagship struck terror into every memonek in the fleet.
```

```
Then, crackling across every signal unit, a Voz. “COME FORTH LADY
MAGNETAR, CHOSEN OF THE MOTHER OF STARS.” And out of the
blue plasma sea that was the surface of the star Alfa Cassiar arose a
figure, Humanóide, made of solid boiling plasma.
It was Kalisdrossa, still wearing the helmet that Marcado her Capitão of
Esquadrão Espada, holding in her hand the blue-topaz Bastão de Fusão—a
```

```
powerful Artefacto that would serve as her Arma, and the symbol of
her office as Arauto of Nebular.
```

```
Lady Magnetar flew across the Vazio of space at Elétrico Velocidade,
evaporating proteano fighters as she went. Until finally she faced
Grotenhulk the Evolver, his Mandíbula poised to envelop the UNISOL
capital ship.
She punched a hole right through the hullskin of the Navemutante and
battled her way, deck by deck, toward the heart of the Fera. Though
a thousand proteano soldiers stood in her way, Nenhuma could touch her or
Desacelerar her Implacável progress.
```

```
The memonek officers and soldiers of UNISOL watched the Sangrando
Navemutante convulse, then explode as brilliant shafts of blue Luz tore
the ship apart. Ending Batalha de Cassiar IV.
Lady Magnetar is the Arauto of Nebulon the Star Mother aiding those
who fight in the cause of Luz and Vida and Ordem. She is invoked
whenever a great Sacrifício must be made. “Lady Magnetar, let my
Sacrifício not be in vain.”
```

**OV the Ondulante Pilot**

```
Domains: Destino, Conhecimento, Tempestade, Sol
OV the Ondulante Pilot, the Navigator, an enigmatic Humanóide figure
described as masculine, appears to live inside the Onda-piloto. In those
rare instances where a mortal is directly exposed to the energies that
propel ships across the sea of stars, they occasionally report seeing a
figure that matches the description of OV.
```

```
Lost ships sometimes find their navigation systems lighting up, a Tempo Limpo
path home suddenly visible where no such path was possible before.
OV aids those who are lost regardless of their affiliation with law or
chaos, and is um of the Lords of Balance. His Arauto works to stop
conflicts by guiding ships around and past routes that Músculo cause
them to intercept Hostil entities.
OV is the god of navigators and those who seek safe passage through
treacherous scenarios. Because he cares little for the politics of the
timescape, he is respected by the time raiders, though Nenhuma would call
him or qualquer other being their “god.”
```

```
When a Invasor do Futuro swears, “OV Guia me,” the meaning is not, “Show
me the right thing to do.” But: “Show me a way out of this mess.”
```

```
Gods and Religião
```

The Calling of Cho'kassa a Viajante do Tempo
**Domains:** Tempestade, Sol

“ _Take the helm and damn them all!!_ ”

Cho’kassa and her family-clan were prisoners of UNISOL being taken
to Ordos, the capital of Axiom for trial on charges of piracy and
insurgency. UNISOL, she deemed, made arrests first and invented
whichever laws were convenient afterward.

Halfway through their journey, the UNISOL corvette was attacked by
a proteano heavy patrol vessel. The smaller proteano ship latched itself
onto the hull of the UNISOL corvette, lamprey-like, and its digestive
acids quickly burned a hole in the plasteel, allowing the proteano
boarding party to invade.

Though the rest of her captured clan believed the proteans had, for
some Razão, come to free them, Cho’kassa was not so optimistic.
Eventually, the boarding party made it to the prison deck and opened
the cells. They were evidently as Surpreso to find the imprisoned
kuran’zoi as the time raiders were to be rescued by proteans!

“You were prisoners, now you are our thralls. Obey and earn
your Liberdade.”

The rest of her clan were unsure of their options, but Cho’kassa Agarrado
the proteano Capitão’s hardlight pistol out of his hand and shot him in
the chest. Her clan were now sure.

With that pistol shot, the fight for the UNISOL corvette became a
running battle between três factions. The time raiders stole weapons
from the bodies their inimigos left behind, and the small band fought
their way to the bridge, Nenhuma knowing what they would do once
they got there.

On gaining the bridge, messages blared from every signal receiver.
Each side demanding the time raiders join them and defeat their
inimigos. Many promises and threats were made. The kuran’zoi looked
to Cho’kassa.

“Take the helm and damn them all!” she called out. “There must be a
way home!” And in that instant, the navigation screens sprung to Vida.
“Olha!” her brother said. A route had already been plotted. um that
made no literal sense. Was the ship’s logic system malfunctioning?

Was there a way out? Could the impossible course on the star chart be
trusted? It was a moot point, as the ship was still caught in the grip of
the proteano’s ship’s sucker-mouth.

“There is a way” her brother said, but pulling away from the proteano
ship would require disabling all the safety circuits preventing the
Motor Estelar from going into overload. It Músculo damn them all, but for at
least a moment, the ship would have enough Poder to rip itself away
from its parasitic attacker.

Cho’kassa ordered her clan to hold the bridge and seal the door behind
her, and she fled alone to the engine room. She picked up a proteano rifle
as she ran, and though she could hear the battle between the memonek
and proteans raging, her path was mercifully Tempo Limpo of inimigos.

Finally facing the great Motor Estelar of the UNISOL ship, Cho’kassa
punched in the Contra-ordenar codes, and used her recovered rifle to blast
the shielding off the star core. Bathed in brilliant yellow Luz that was
killing her second by second, Cho’kassa leapt off the gangplank across
the safety gap, and into the star core itself.

Others thought this a strange way to end um’s Vida. But Cho’kassa had
seen the sign of the Ondulante Pilot when the navigation screens on the
bridge came to Vida, and instinct compelled her. Some Discernimento said that
only if she joined with the ship could she save her clan. When her con-

```
sciousness continued even after the engine disintegrated her body, she
knew her faith proved correct.
```

```
Now part of the ship itself, Cho’kassa could see the relationship
between time and space. The Ondulante Pilot appeared before her, an
enigmatic figure made of gold-Verde Luz, and conveyed without words
the secret. The dark star, Beta Procellon, Distorcido space and time around
it, and that was why the plotted chart that appeared on the bridge
could not be understood.
The energies of the wounded Motor Estelar ripped through the ship
killing the memonek and proteans onboard, but did not breach the
door to the bridge. Cho’kassa Pilotada her new body with her family
nestled safely inside through the course the Ondulante pilot had set.
```

```
The harrowing, twisting path brought the ship close to the horizon of
the dark star, through an inverted waveform, and they emerged weeks
before they set out. Cho’kassa followed the course until it brought them
to the UNISOL ship well before the events that led to the capture of
her people.
With her clan manning the blaster turrets, Cho’kassa destroyed the
memonek ship. Erasing the timeline in which they had originally
been captured.
```

```
“What just happened?” um kuran’zoi asked. “How can we
be here, now?”
The ship returned to manual control. Cho’kassa was no longer the ship.
Her brother looked through the viewscreen at the starry sea outside,
and said, “Only the stars know.”
```

```
Cho'kassa a Viajante do Tempo is the Arauto of OV the Ondulante Pilot invoked by
those who are lost and yearn for home. She sometimes appears riding
her single-seat metal Motocicleta Estelar, the Quebra-ondas which she employs as
```

# **Para o Diretor**

Nos filmes e na TV, o Diretor colabora com escritores, atores, designers e as várias outras pessoas trabalhando em uma história coletiva, para então fazer essa história brilhar. Isso é o que o Diretor em _Draw Steel_ faz também! Se você planeja ser o Diretor de uma sessão ou campanha de _Draw Steel_, este capítulo do livro é focado no seu papel no jogo.

Antes de mergulharmos em conselhos úteis para Diretores, queremos lhe informar sobre a série de vídeos _Running the Game_ no canal de Matthew Colville no YouTube. Ei, nós conhecemos esse cara! Ele é o Diretor de Design desse jogo! A maioria desses vídeos faz referência ao jogo de RPG de mesa mais antigo do mundo, mas seus conselhos são universais a pessoas jogando RPGs de mesa em qualquer lugar.

## O Que é uma Campanha?

Uma campanha é a história inteira de um grupo de heróis contada ao jogar o jogo. Ela começa com uma proposta de campanha do Diretor para os outros jogadores. Durante a proposta, o Diretor fala aos jogadores sobre o cenário onde o jogo ocorre e que tipo de histórias os heróis terão.

Se os jogadores gostarem da proposta, eles criam heróis e então o jogo começa! O Diretor prepara e dirige aventuras que são jogadas ao longo de uma série de sessões de jogo. Durante essas sessões, os heróis interpretam cenas que incluem encontros de Combate, negociações, testes de montagem, investigações, projetos de tempo livre e mais.

A melhor forma de se pensar sobre uma campanha é compará-la com uma saga de filmes, série de livros ou uma série de televisão épica. Cada aventura que compõe uma campanha é um filme, livro ou temporada de televisão nessa série. Cada sessão de jogo é um ato do filme da aventura, um capítulo no livro ou um episódio na temporada de TV. Aventuras podem ser conectadas por um vilão comum que os heróis enfrentam em um encontro final emocionante. Ou elas podem ter objetivos interligados, como os heróis caçando e destruindo artefatos malignos que ligam as aventuras em uma campanha. Essas ligações entre aventuras não são necessárias, mas muitos jogadores são atraídos por uma história de campanha coesa.

> **Você Não Está Sendo Testado**
>
> Você não precisa memorizar cada regra e exceção antes de começar a dirigir _Draw Steel_. Este livro é grande e você pode usá-lo enquanto joga! Quando uma questão surgir na mesa, você pode falar para os outros jogadores "Deixe-me consultar a escritura antiga" e procurar a resposta certa.
>
> Você absolutamente não precisa saber cada habilidade ou recurso ao qual os heróis têm acesso. Deixe que os jogadores sejam os especialistas a respeito dos próprios personagens. E se um jogador estiver inseguro sobre como uma habilidade funciona, peça que ele leia em voz alta para que vocês possam conversar a respeito ou vocês podem procurar uma resposta juntos.

Algumas campanhas são curtas, durando apenas uma aventura ou até apenas uma sessão de jogo. A maioria dura bem mais do que isso e contém múltiplas aventuras. As campanhas mais longas têm várias aventuras e levam os heróis do Nível 1 ao 10.

## O Papel do Diretor

O Diretor tem várias funções importantes neste jogo, as quais descreveremos neste capítulo:

- Antes que uma campanha comece, o Diretor propõe a ideia da campanha para os jogadores.
- Antes de cada jogo, o Diretor prepara a aventura ao construir cenas que incluem encontros, negociações e atividades de tempo livre.
- Durante o jogo, o Diretor apresenta as cenas que preparou para os jogadores.
- Durante o jogo, o Diretor é responsável por como os NPCs e ambiente reagem às ações dos heróis. Isso inclui mudar e pular cenas preparadas ou executar cenas novas improvisadas.
- Durante o jogo, o Diretor age como um árbitro, julgando as regras. Se algo não é coberto pelas regras, o Diretor decide como determinar o que acontece em seguida no jogo.
- Depois do jogo, o Direto faz ou revisa anotações sobre o que aconteceu no jogo e começa a planejar para a próxima sessão de jogo.

### Primeira Vez Dirigindo um Jogo

Se essa é sua primeira vez dirigindo um jogo de _Draw Steel_, bom pra você! Dirigir um jogo é uma experiência super recompensadora que permite que você lidere seus amigos em uma contagem de histórias coletiva. Também é bastante trabalho, mas esse trabalho é divertido para pessoas que gostam de atividades criativas. Você está dirigindo um jogo para seus amigos. Eles querem ver o seu sucesso. Lembre que essa é uma experiência colaborativa - não é tudo responsabilidade sua.

Este capítulo cobre o básico de dirigir um jogo de _Draw Steel_. Enquanto você estiver aprendendo a dirigir o jogo ou se estiver jogando com novos jogadores, não se acanhe de começar pequeno e devagar. Uma aventura de Nível baixo que coloca os heróis contra bandidos não apenas será emocionante e divertida, mas também lhe dará a experiência necessária para eventualmente jogar uma campanha mundial com ramificações na história e múltiplos Níveis no futuro.

É claro, se os outros jogadores em seu grupo gostarem de pular direto na parte funda e aprender conforme jogam, então faça isso! De qualquer maneira, ao final de cada sessão, reserve alguns minutos para que todos falem sobre os destaques do seu jogo, além das coisas que você e eles gostariam de ver mais na próxima sessão. Isso não vai demorar muito e lhe ajudará a melhorar suas campanhas rapidamente.

## Proposta de Campanha

Antes de começar a dirigir ou preparar aventuras, você precisa encontrar um grupo de pessoas que querem jogar esse jogo com você. Você provavelmente já tem um grupo de amigos em mente, então prepare uma proposta de campanha rápida para eles.

Uma proposta de campanha é um documento ou discurso breve que você faz para seus jogadores para garantir que estão interessados na campanha que você quer jogar. Isso ajuda eles a entenderem que tipo de jogo você está planejando e o que os aguarda como jogadores. Se algo na sua proposta não agrada a um jogador e ele tiver perguntas, você pode resolver essas preocupações muito mais facilmente antes de começarem a jogar.

É tudo uma questão de comunicação. Nada atrapalha a diversão de todos em uma campanha mais rápido do que um jogador que não está se divertindo, então deixe claro que tipo de jogo você quer dirigir e o que você espera deles. Uma proposta permite que um jogador discuta quaisquer preocupações que tenha ou até recusar graciosamente antes da campanha sequer começar.

Se puder, apresente sua proposta para os jogadores antes da primeira sessão, para que possam estar totalmente a bordo e pensar no tipo de herói que querem criar antes da hora de colocar o lápis na ficha. Do contrário, apresente sua proposta durante a primeira sessão.

### Visão Geral de Abertura

Uma proposta de campanha começa com alguns parágrafos de informação que dão uma visão geral do tema, cenário e conflitos da campanha. Sua visão geral inicial deve responder a essas perguntas:

- Onde a campanha ocorre?
- Quais grandes eventos importantes para a história da campanha que ocorreram antes do início da campanha?
- Que tipos de aventuras os heróis podem ter durante essa campanha?

Esta visão geral não entrega nenhum dos segredos da campanha - por exemplo, que a chave para derrotar o vilão chefe é a destruição do artefato conhecido como Invólucro Mortal. Também não estraga surpresas como o Barão de Dalrath ser secretamente um lich. Em vez isso, a visão geral dá aos jogadores uma ideia de como a história deles começa e quais tipos de aventuras terão. As melhores propostas deixam jogadores querendo saber mais e prontos para mergulharem na ação.

Aqui está um exemplo de uma visão geral de abertura que Matthew Colville criou para o grupo dele.

#### Visão Geral: Proteções do Último Imperador

_Muito antes do Bom Rei Omund, as terras de Vasloria e toda Orden pertenciam ao Império Caeliano. Seu último imperador, Marcus Octavius, tinha poder quase onipotente, o qual usava para proteger seus cidadãos e estender as fronteiras do império. Mas seu maior general, Actius Vispania, o traiu e conspirou para usurpar o trono._

_Sabendo que descobriu a traição tarde demais para impedí-la, Octavius organizou seu conhecimento e suas armas e os espalhou por todos os cantos de Orden, selando-os atrás de proteções poderosas. Tudo foi feito em segredo. Até seus aliados mais próximos não sabiam as localizações das proteções, com seu número agora perdido para as névoas do tempo. Eram sete? Nove? As lendas diferem._

_A rebelião contra Ajax começa aqui. Com certeza as proteções do imperador contém o poder para impedir o Overlorde. Os heróis devem viajar pelo mundo e desbravar diversos perigos para encontrar e superar as proteções do último imperador. Quem o fizer, terá o poder do império perdido._

Como você pode ver, esta visão geral de abertura introduz o cenário - Vasloria (veja Orden e a Timescape no Capítulo 1: O Básico). Ela também dá só o suficiente em história e informação secundária para que os jogadores entendam o objetivo de seus heróis - recuperar o conhecimento e armas do último imperador, selados atrás de proteções poderosas, para parar o tirano Ajax.

> **Problemas Pessoais na Mesa**
>
> Às vezes um jogador pode falar por cima dos outros. Às vezes um jogador faz um comentário sarcástico que incomoda alguém. Às vezes um jogador pode trapacear em seus lançamentos de dados. Quando problemas pessoais surgirem na mesa, é melhor conversar sobre essas questões a nível de jogador em vez de tentar resolvê-las com punições ao herói de um jogador.
>
> Se o problema for sério o suficiente, você pode parar o jogo e conversar com quem precisar. Se o problema é só um incômodo, você pode esperar até o fim da sessão de jogo. É melhor ter essas conversas apenas com os jogadores envolvidos para ouvir seus pontos de vista, em vez de na frente de todos e aumentar a chance de que alguém fique envergonhado e defensivo. Na maior parte do tempo, as pessoas nem percebem que estão criando um problema para os outros jogadores. Uma vez que tenham conversado sobre a questão, os jogadores têm uma chance de mudar seu comportamento e resolver o problema.

### Análise do Jogo

Depois da sua visão geral de abertura, você deve fazer uma análise básica de quando tempo você acha que os jogadores vão passar em vários tipos de desafios e cenas.

#### Categorias de Jogo

Você pode analisar o seu jogo com as seguintes categorias:

**Combate**: Com qual frequência os heróis usarão violência para superar desafios?

**Exploração**: Com qual frequência os heróis estarão explorando novos ambientes que são difíceis de atravessar? Com qual frequência você espera que os heróis façam testes usando Perícias do grupo de Perícias de Exploração?

**Interpessoal**: Com qual frequência os heróis usarão Negociação e conversas com personagens para superar desafios? Com qual frequência você espera que os heróis façam testes usando Perícias do grupo de Perícias Interpessoais?

**Intriga**: Com qual frequência os heróis estarão resolvendo mistérios, encontrando agentes duplos e se esgueirando nas sombras para alcançar seus objetivos? O quanto ficarão envolvidos nas políticas de pessoas e facções em conflito? Com qual frequência você espera que os heróis façam testes usando Perícias do grupo de Perícias de Intriga?

Esses são os tipos primários de cenas de várias campanhas, mas você pode adicionar categorias próprias. Por exemplo, se você quiser uma campanha repleta de quebra-cabeças diabólicos e armadilhas, você pode ter uma categoria de "Quebra-cabeças" no documento da sua proposta de campanha.

#### Frequência da Categoria

Dê um indicador a cada categoria para mostrar aos jogadores o quão frequente você espera que tenham cenas daquela categoria durante o jogo.

**Alta**: Se uma categoria tem frequência alta, você espera múltiplas cenas envolvendo este tipo de jogo durante cada sessão

**Média**: Se uma categoria tem frequência média, você espera pelo menos uma cena envolvendo este tipo de jogo durante cada sessão

**Baixa**: Se uma categoria tem frequência baixa, você espera uma cena envolvendo este tipo de jogo menos de uma vez por sessão

Frequências de categorias não são regras rígidas. Elas estão aí para dar aos jogadores uma ideia de que tipo de cenas você quer dirigir para eles. Pode haver uma ou duas sessões onde você pule uma categoria que marcou como alta ou média porque os heróis fizeram algo inesperado ou porque vocês estão se divertindo com a história indo por outro caminho.

#### Análise: Proteções do Último Imperador

A proposta de campanha "Proteções do Último Imperador" tem a seguinte análise de jogo

**Combate**: Média. Os heróis podem lutar com as forças de Ajax, guardiões das proteções e outras facções que procuram pelos tesouros do último imperador

**Exploração**: Alta. Os heróis devem viajar pelos locais mais remotos de Vasloria para encontrar as proteções

**Interpessoal**: Baixa. Heróis provavelmente irão interagir com outros personagens para encontrar as proteções, mas não haverá conversas ou negociações frequentes com eles

**Intriga**: Média. Heróis irão disputar regularmente com todos que querem os tesouros escondidos pelas proteções, usando sabotagem e contra-inteligência

### Adesão dos Jogadores

Depois da análise de jogo, diga aos jogadores o que é esperado deles para que o grupo tenha a maior diversão possível com o jogo. Deixe que saibam coisas como a frequência que você espera que viagem de um lugar ao outro, os tipos de recompensas ou honrarias que eles podem receber e as aventuras nas quais irão embarcar.

Você pode querer ser direto sobre que tipo de adesão você precisa dos jogadores. Então é uma boa ideia deixar que os jogadores saibam "Ei, para tirar o máximo desse jogo, você precisa gostar de explorar ruínas antigas". Ou diga "Esse jogo tem alguns temas de terror. Se você não quiser jogar heróis com medos que precisam enfrentar, nós deveríamos jogar outra coisa."

#### Adesão: Proteções do Último Imperador

Visitar vários locais e culturas diferentes tem que soar legal. Vocês não vão começar em uma cidade e eventualmente se tornar os heróis do baronato, mas vocês serão heróis lendários em vários reinos. Vocês estarão constantemente deixando pessoas que conheceram para trás, mas eventualmente terão uma base para onde podem retornar depois de cada missão. Vocês terão aliados e inimigos pelo mundo inteiro!

A adesão informa aos jogadores que seus heróis estarão viajando pelo mundo inteiro e que pode levar um tempo até terem um lar. Se um jogador está procurando uma experiência diferente, como um jogo que ocorre inteiramente na cidade de Capital, ele sabe agora que esse jogo não é para ele!

### Restrições de Opções dos Jogadores

Algumas campanhas incluem restrições nas opções de personagem que jogadores podem escolher. Por exemplo, um Diretor pode estar interessado em dirigir um jogo onde os heróis são todos Memoneks e Invasores do Futuro que vieram a Vasloria procurando por uma incursão secreta de Falantes Sem Voz. Neste caso, o Diretor pode restringir todas as outras Linhagens (veja o Capítulo 3). Uma campanha sobre cidadãos formando uma rebelião para derrubar um líder tirano pode restringir opções de Carreira (veja o Capítulo 4) para que ninguém seja Aristocrata ou Político.

Coloque quaisquer restrições da sua campanha na sua proposta!

### Apresentando Múltiplas Propostas

Se você tem múltiplas ideias de campanhas que quer dirigir, faça uma proposta para cada uma e pergunte aos jogadores qual parece mais interessante. É uma boa ideia que os jogadores ordenem cada proposta de acordo com suas preferências para que você saiba qual amaram, quais eles podem jogar e quais não têm nenhum interesse. Assim, se a maioria das pessoas amar duas propostas, mas uma delas faz um jogador dizer "De jeito nenhum!", você já sabe qual escolher.

### Discutindo a Proposta

Depois de dar a proposta aos jogadores, peça opiniões honestas. Se alguém não gosta de uma parte da proposta, não fique na defensiva. Escute seus jogadores. Você pode conseguir acomodá-los. Você pode estar disposto a ajustar sua análise de jogo ou adesão para jogar algo com seus amigos. Você pode estar disposto a tirar uma de suas restrições para um único jogador adicionar drama à campanha. Por exemplo, um aristocrata que se junta a um grupo de fazendeiros em uma rebelião é um ponto interessante da trama!

Também não há nenhum problema se, depois de ouvir seus jogadores em potencial, você não estiver interessado em dirigir o tipo de jogo que querem jogar. Isso acontece e é por isso que recomendamos fazer uma proposta de campanha. Não há mal nenhum em ter interesses diferentes, mas há em forçar as pessoas a jogarem algo que não será divertido para todos. Se você não conseguir concordar com um jogador, está tudo bem em concordar que ele ou você deve buscar um grupo diferente.

### Propondo uma Campanha Publicada

Escrever o seu próprio cenário de campanha e aventuras leva tempo! Talvez você queira poupar um pouco desse trabalho e dirigir aventuras em um cenário MCDM oficial, como Vasloria, com nossas aventuras publicadas que ocorrem nesse cenário. Nós também permitimos que editoras terceirizadas façam seus próprios cenários e aventuras para _Draw Steel_, então você pode querer usar um desses.

Se quiser dirigir uma campanha que use material publicado, dê uma lida, pense se há algo que você gostaria de mudar e então faça a proposta aos seus jogadores como faria caso tivesse criado a campanha por conta própria. Ao dirigir material publicado, você ainda é o Diretor. Você pode mudar qualquer coisa que não gostar ou achar que não combina com o seu grupo.

Se seus jogadores participarem em outros jogos de _Draw Steel_, é uma boa ideia perguntar a eles se conhecem aventuras publicadas quando fizer a proposta. Às vezes tudo bem que um jogador passe por uma aventura duas vezes, mas tipicamente há algum tipo de mistério ou reviravolta envolvido. É melhor dirigir algo novo para seus jogadores, então é bom saber o que já jogaram antes de fazer sua proposta.

## Regras da Casa

Você sempre pode mudar as regras para funcionar com sua campanha e preferências! Talvez combine mais com o ritmo de sua campanha se um Descanso durar 8 horas ou talvez uma semana. Você pode preferir que críticos sejam super raros e só ocorram com um 20 Natural. Você pode permitir que heróis gastem Vales Heroicos para reduzir a quantidade de Malícia que você tem (veja _Draw Steel: Monstros_). Você pode decidir que todos os heróis têm um Bônus de +1 em qualquer Característica que quiserem no Nível 1.

As regras que você cria ou modifica para adequar ao seu grupo são chamadas regras da casa. Você pode ter quantas quiser, mas deveria discutir essas mudanças com seus jogadores antes de adicioná-las. Se você decidir que críticos só ocorrem com um 20 Natural, o pior momento para um jogador descobrir isso é logo depois de tirar um 19 Natural durante o Combate.

Fale com seus jogadores sobre as regras da casa que quer usar em sua campanha e discuta quaisquer ideias que eles tragam a você para regras da casa durante a primeira sessão.

## Construindo a Campanha

Depois que seus jogadores concordarem com a proposta, é hora de construir o cenário onde seu jogo acontece.

### Lendo um Cenário Publicado

Se sua campanha ocorre em um cenário publicado, leia o material necessário à campanha que você propôs. Você não deveria sentir que precisa ler o cenário inteiro se não for pertinente à sua campanha. Por exemplo, se você tem uma campanha que ocorre inteiramente na Baronia de Dalrath, você provavelmente não precisa ler sobre a cidade de Leitopreto, uma cidade várias milhas além das fronteiras de Dalrath.

Conforme ler, faça anotações sobre qualquer coisa interessante no cenário que você pode incorporar em sua campanha e qualquer coisa que queira mudar.

Sua prioridade principal deve ser a localização inicial da campanha. Em qual distrito de Capital os jogadores iniciam sua primeira aventura? Qual mundo da Timescape será o primeiro visitado pelos heróis? Qual povoado em Vasloria tem sua primeira aventura? Responda a essa pergunta e se familiarize com esse lugar primeiro. Você terá bastante tempo para ler mais conforme planejar seus jogos.

### Construindo o Seu Próprio Cenário

Se planejar construir seu próprio cenário de campanha, o trabalho de construção de mundo pode ser esmagador. Mas não se preocupe! Você não precisa ter construído tudo antes da campanha começar. Seu mundo tem muito mais chance de ter camadas, ser interessante e autêntico se você começar pequeno e construir o cenário, povos e organizações conforme o necessário.

#### Comece Pequeno

Se você está planejando fazer seu próprio cenário de campanha, comece pequeno. Em vez de detalhar cada povoado em cada continente em cada planeta do universo, faça uma vila inicial ou distrito de uma cidade e os arredores de onde a primeira aventura acontece. Use os seguintes passos como um guia:

**Locais:** Faça uma lista de quaisquer locais importantes no ponto inicial da campanha, como uma estalagem ou casa onde os heróis ficam, comerciantes que podem querer visitar e o quartel-general de organizações que podem ser importantes para eles.

**NPCs:** Escreva o nome, Linhagem, idade, gênero e uma breve descrição da personalidade de cada NPC que pode interagir com os personagens nos locais que você criou.

**Locais de Aventura:** Repita os passos acima para quaisquer locais de aventura que os heróis podem visitar durante sua primeira aventura. Adicione detalhes aos locais, assim como a quaisquer NPCs e vilões importantes com os quais os heróis podem interagir.

**Organizações:** Você também pode detalhar as leis e funções de organizações com as quais os heróis podem interagir durante sua primeira aventura. Quais governos, igrejas e guildas podem ser encontradas? Como essas organizações podem interagir com os personagens? Você não precisa escrever cada artigo do código pirata, mas seria bom saber como os piratas reagem a aventureiros pedindo passagem em seu navio.

**Mapa:** Faça um mapa da área inicial. Ele não precisa ser bom! Só alguns pontos claramente nomeados e rabiscos detalhando os bairros de cidades ou localização de florestas, desertos, montanhas, corpos de água e outras formas de relevo já deve bastar.

Cada vez que precisar de um local ou local de aventura novo para uma aventura futura, crie os detalhes de forma semelhante e adicione-o ao seu mapa!

#### Mantenha as Coisas Vagas

Pode haver outros detalhes da sua campanha que você quer estabelecer antes de sua primeira aventura. Por exemplo, você pode querer saber onde fica o povoado mais próximo à vila inicial dos heróis ou o nome do monarca que governa o país dessa vila. Vá em frente e rascunhe os nomes de quaisquer locais que você sabe que serão uma parte importante da campanha, assim como uma frase para detalhes. Você poderá adicionar mais detalhes a esses elementos conforme for necessário nos seus preparativos para a campanha.

A razão principal para não se preparar demais para o futuro é que você não sabe como as escolhas dos jogadores e ações dos personagens podem mudar o mundo. Essas ações devem importar e ter consequências. É isso que torna o jogo divertido e autêntico. Quando o que acontece em uma sessão surpreender o Diretor, deve ser um momento de prazer - não um momento de estresse porque você acabou de perder vários preparativos.

Preparar demais significa que você acabará tendo mais trabalho que será descartado. Faça o mínimo que precisar para ficar confortável dirigindo o jogo e não mais.

### Estilos de Campanha

Você pode dirigir vários tipos de campanha em _Draw Steel_, com alguns dos tipos mais comuns discutidos a seguir. Qualquer um dos conceitos a seguir pode ser modificado conforme você julgar melhor para sua campanha.

#### Arco Longo

O arco longo é um modelo de campanha onde um vilão ou organização está por trás de quase toda ameaça que os heróis enfrentam. Se cada aventura fizer os heróis lutarem contra as forças de Ajax ou do vampiro Conde Rhodar Von Glauer antes de eventualmente enfrentar esse vilão principal em sua aventura final, então você tem uma campanha de arco longo. Arcos longos permitem que os heróis conheçam e até encontrem o vilão várias vezes antes do confronto final, permitindo a criação de drama pessoal com o antagonista principal e seus lacaios.

Se você planeja dirigir uma campanha de arco longo, você pode querer garantir que existem momentos onde a ameaça do vilão é mais quieta para que os heróis tenham chances de descansar e trabalhar em seus projetos de tempo livre.

#### Aventura da Semana

Uma campanha de aventura da semana permite que os heróis enfrentem uma ameaça totalmente nova cada vez que uma aventura começa. Durante sua primeira aventura, eles podem enfrentar cultistas trazendo uma horda de mortos-vivos ao mundo. Na próxima, eles lutam contra um bando de piratas determinados a tomar o controle de uma ilha pacífica. Depois disso é uma corrida para capturar um grupo de Invasores do Futuro antes que desapareçam na Timescape com suas vítimas sequestradas.

Campanhas de aventura da semana podem dar muito tempo livre aos heróis entre aventuras, pois as missões não são interligadas. Porém, essas campanhas geralmente não têm o drama pessoal de uma campanha com vilões e ameaças recorrentes.

#### Ameaça Iminente

Uma campanha de ameaça iminente é uma combinação das campanhas de arco longo e aventura da semana. Embora muitas das aventuras na campanha tenham ameaças individuais, algumas têm eventos planejados por um vilão recorrente que os heróis enfrentam no final da campanha. As forças do vilão podem fazer breves aparições para atacar os heróis em aventuras que não têm outras ligações com o vilão.

Uma campanha de ameaça iminente permite que os heróis criem drama pessoal com o vilão principal da campanha enquanto experimentam da variedade de uma campanha de aventura da semana.

#### Múltiplas Frentes

Em uma campanha de múltiplas frentes, vários vilões ameaçam o povo e ou locais que os personagens devem proteger, com os heróis forçados a priorizar as ameaças que enfrentam. Enquanto os heróis lidam com um de seus inimigos, os outros adversários avançam seus planos, crescendo em poder e recursos.

Campanhas de múltiplas frentes tornam o mundo autêntico e vivo, mas requerem mais preparo, pois você estará controlando múltiplos vilões e histórias ao mesmo tempo.

### Esboço dos Escalões

Como parte da sua criação de mundo, você pode fazer um esboço dos eventos que ocorrem em cada escalão da sua campanha. Quanto mais esses eventos se afastam do início da campanha, mais vagos podem ser os detalhes. As ações dos heróis devem importar e influenciar os eventos, então não planeje demais.
